如上所述，一般来说，更高层次的关系，特别是秩序的组成，长期以来对系统论者提出了一些挑战(例如，Davis & Heywood，1963年) ，秩序的限制比家庭的限制更加不稳定。像 Apiales、 Crossosomatales 和潘达纳莱斯这样的宗派组合是绝对出乎意料的，然而，这些更高层次的宗派甚至在不同分类哲学的作品中也被普遍接受(一个很好的例子是海伍德等人2007年的作品)。然而，在诸如 Malpighiales、 Asparagales 等国家中，寻找特色人物的尝试基本上都失败了(见 Endress & Matthews 2006a)。但是，与科一样，分子研究所建议的分类可能会得到形态学和/或化学特征的支持。因此，拥有属性目解剖了它们的种皮，而 Pittosporaceae 和伞形科/五加科之间独特的化学相似性早已为人所知(Hegnauer 1969b 参考文献)。随着我们对形态学和化学知识的提高，我们可以希望逐步改进分支特征和检测各个层次上的畸形。

The discovery of the relationships of parasitic and aquatic groups in particular have presented a challenge to systematists. Morphologically, some of these plants are so highly modified that interpretation of the plant body in conventional terms is difficult or even impossible. Thus parasitic groups such as Rafflesiaceae are hard to place since both the vegetative body and the flowers are changed almost beyond recognition (see Naumann et al. 2013: comprehensive study of parasitic taxa and their evolution). The same is true, although to a lesser extent, in many plants pollinated by wind, etc.; a variety of characters may be affected, and wind-pollinated plants have independently acquired similar modifications. Morphological change is also extensive in mycoheterotrophic/sapromycotrophic (Leake 1994) and carnivorous groups. Again, in the latter there are limited number of morphologies (e.g. pitcher leaves, sticky glandular hairs) involved in the carnivorous habit, and there may even be convergence at the molecular level, as in the convergent evolution of digestive enzymes (Fukushima et al. 2017), while mycoheterotrophic monocots from three orders clustered together in an analysis by Lam et al. (2018) because of long branch attraction in the molecular data.

特别是发现寄生生物和水生生物之间的关系，对系统学家提出了挑战。在形态学上，这些植物中的一些是如此高度地改变，以至于用传统的术语来解释植物体是困难的，甚至是不可能的。因此，象花卉科这样的寄生类群很难定位，因为营养体和花朵都几乎变得无法辨认(见 Naumann 等人2013年: 寄生类群及其进化的综合研究)。同样的情况也是如此，尽管程度较轻，在许多通过风传粉的植物中，等等; 各种性状可能受到影响，风传粉的植物也独立获得了类似的变异。真菌异养/腐真菌营养(Leake 1994)和肉食性群体的形态变化也很广泛。同样，在后者中，肉食习性涉及的形态结构(例如瓶状叶、粘性腺毛)数量有限，甚至可能在分子水平上有聚集，如在消化酶的趋同演化中(福岛等人，2017年) ，而来自3个目的真菌异养单子叶聚集在一起由 Lam 等人(2018年)的分析，因为分子数据中的长枝吸引效应。

In molecular analyses of parasitic groups, plastid gene sequences may be difficult or impossible to obtain, the chloroplast DNA in particular experiencing extensive gene loss. Gene loss seems to have occured in parallel (independently in the different groups), yet a core of functional genes remains, probably because of functional constraints (Delannoy et al. 2011). In parasitic plants the rate of molecular change in general is often high (e.g. Duff & Nickrent 1997; Nickrent et al. 1998; Caddick et al. 2002a; G. Petersen et al. 2006b; Barkman et al. 2007; Bromham et al. 2103), and the inclusion of parasitic taxa in molecular analyses can cause conniptions (e.g. Nickrent et al. 2004; Davis et al. 2004; Chase et al. 2006; G. Petersen et al. 2006b), not least because there can be horizontal transmission of genes (e.g. Davis & Wurdack 2005: Vitaceae to Rafflesiaceae; Barkman et al. 2007: the mitochondrial *atp*1 gene commonly moves) including the the invasive *cox*1 intron (Barkman et al. 2007).

在寄生群体的分子分析中，质体基因序列可能很难或不可能获得，特别是叶绿体 DNA 经历了广泛的基因丢失。基因损失似乎是平行发生的(在不同的群体中独立发生) ，然而功能基因的核心保留下来，可能是因为功能限制(delanew 等人，2011年)。在寄生植物中，分子变化的速度通常很快(例如，Duff & Nickrent 1997; Nickrent et al. 1998; Caddick et al. 2002 a; g. Petersen et al. 2006 b; Barkman et al. 2007; 布朗厄姆 et al. 2103) ，在分子分析中纳入分类群可能导致寄生虫的死亡(例如: Nickrent et al. 2004; Davis et al. 2004; Chase et al. 2006; g. Petersen et al. 2006 b)不仅仅是因为可能存在水平传播基因(例如 Davis & Wurdack 2005: Vitaceae to Rafflesiaceae; Barkman et al. 2007: the mtdna atp1 gene common moves) ，包括侵入性的 cox1 intron (Barkman et al. 2007)。

Progress is being made: placements for Rafflesiaceae, Mitrastemonaceae, Cytinaceae and Cynomoriaceae have been suggested (Barkman et al. 2004; Davis & Wurdack 2004; Nickrent et al. 2004; Davis et al. 2007; Bellot et al. 2016), and although it seems likely that Burmanniaceae s.l. are polyphyletic, the parts are all to be located in Dioscoreales (Merckx et al. 2006, 2009a, 2010a). Similarly, in the aquatic habitat neither vessels in particular nor much xylem in general is needed; leaves are highly modified; and water-mediated pollination, if adopted, may well be associated with major changes in floral morphology. Here, too, molecular studies suggest that aquatic groups with hitherto problematic relationships may find homes. Thus Podostemaceae are close to Calophyllaceae and Hypericaceae (Malpighiales: e.g. Kita & Kato 2001; Ruhfel et al. 2011, 2013), Hydatellaceae, which used to be in Poales, are part of Nymphaeales (Saarela et al. 2007), and Hydrostachyaceae have a similar relationship with Cornales (Xiang et al. 2002; Schäferhoff et al. 2010; Xiang et al. 2011), although they have been placed in Lamiales (Burleigh et al. 2009). In the first two cases in particular there are morphological and chemical features that support the movse. Very different placements of Ceratophyllaceae have beeen suggested over the years, unfortunately, its relationships still remain uncertain (e.g. Doyle et al. 2015; Kvacek et al. 2016 and references). If Ceratophyllaceae are sister to eudicots (e.g. Moore et al. 2007), they are so derived that there is no morphological evidence of which I am aware to support this relationship. Needless to say, as relationships for such wind-pollinated, parasitic, etc., taxa, are clarified, it changes one's understanding of evolution, both of the groups themselves (e.g. Hardy & Cook 2012)and the clades in which they find new homes.

目前正在取得进展: 已经提出了植入花梗科、石菖蒲科、莎草科和锁骨科的建议(Barkman 等人，2004; Davis & Wurdack，2004; Nickrent 等人，2004; Davis 等人，2007; Bellot 等人，2016) ，虽然看起来很可能是多植物科，这些部分都位于 Dioscoreales (Merckx 等人，2006,2009a，2010a)。同样，在水生生境中，既不需要特别的导管，也不需要一般的木质部; 叶子经过高度修饰; 如果采用水介导授粉，很可能与花形态的重大变化有关。在这里，分子研究也表明，迄今为止关系有问题的水生群体可能会找到家园。因此，广藿香科与山茱萸科和山茱萸科(山茱萸科: 如北和加藤2001年; Ruhfel 等人2011年，2013年)很接近，山茱萸科，曾经在 Poales，是 Nymphaeales 的一部分(Saarela 等人2007年) ，山茱萸科与山茱萸目有类似的关系(Xiang 等人2002年; Schäferhoff 等人2010年; Xiang 等人2011年) ，虽然它们已经被放置在 Lamiales (Burleigh 等人2009年)。特别是在前两种情况下，有形态学和化学特征支持运动。这些年来，金鱼藻科植物的位置已经发生了很大的变化，不幸的是，它们之间的关系仍然不确定(例如: Doyle 等人2015; Kvacek 等人2016和参考文献)。如果金鱼藻科是真子叶植物的近亲(例如 Moore 等人2007年) ，那么它们是如此的衍生以至于没有形态学上的证据来支持这种关系。不用说，随着风媒传粉、寄生等物种之间的关系得到澄清，人们对进化的理解也会发生改变，包括这两个物种本身(例如 Hardy & Cook 2012)以及它们在其中找到新家的分支。

In many cases the "new" family limits of the Angiosperm Phylogeny Group (see A.P.G. 1999, 2003, 2009, 2016) are not really controversial, although changes from the limits commonly accepted only a decade ago are sometimes quite dramatic (e.g. Wagenitz 1997). Thus the split of the old Saxifragaceae s.l. is necessitated by its extreme polyphyly, as also with Icacinaceae and Cornaceae. Although such groups had long been considered unsatisfactory, there had been no compelling evidence allowing the user to prefer one circumscription over another; now there is. It is generally accepted that the limits of Lamiaceae and Verbenaceae have to be redrawn, and the content of the two has changed considerably, and they are now easier to identify than before. Hence the decision to recognise the recircumscribed families is not difficult, and if they were not kept separate, much of Lamiales would collapse into a single family. The same is true for Salicaceae and Achariaceae (Malpighiales), two previously small families that have received the bulk of the old Flacourtiaceae. Clade and hence taxon limits do remain difficult in some Malpighiales, but even there clade support is strengthening (Xi et al. 2012b). Euphorbiaceae have presented problems - in the past, one could recognise Euphorbiaceae s.l. quite easily because of their explosively-dehiscent fruits with a distinctive persistent columella. Putranjivaceae, one quite unrelated segregate, are quite distinct, as is confirmed by chemical evidence (presence of glucosinolates/mustard oils), but there are four families that make up the bulk of the old Euphorbiaceae that remain in the same part of the Malpighiales tree (e.g. Wurdack et al. 2004; Davis et al. 2005). However, there is no molecular evidence warranting combining just these Euphorbiaceae segregates, and if they were to come together, the clades in this part of the tree suggest novel groupings not recognised before. Thus Rafflesiaceae appear to be embedded within the single-ovulate ex-Euphorbiaceae (Davis et al. 2007), and there is little enthusiasm for reducing the iconic Rafflesiaceae to synonymy. In the sister clade are biovulate ex-Euphorbiaceae - and the well-known Linaceae. Relationships in core Caryophyllales, especially around Phytolaccaceae (perhaps somewhat surprisingly) and Molluginaceae (less surprisingly) were incompletely understood and refashioning of taxon limits has continued as relationships become more apparent (see e.g. Nyffeler & Eggli 2010; Christin et al. 2011a; Brockington et al. 2011; Y. Yang et al. 2015; Christenhusz et al. 2014). The old Icacinaceae have been broken up (see in particular Stull et al. 2015), however, clade limits in the old Olacaceae, mostly hemiparasites, remain unclear (Nickrent et al. 2010 and references).

在许多情况下，被子植物种系发生学组的“新”家族界限(参见 a.p.g. 1999,2003,2009,2016)并不是真正有争议的，尽管与十年前普遍接受的界限相比的变化有时相当戏剧性(例如 Wagenitz 1997)。因此，老虎耳草科的分裂是必要的，因为它的极端多植物，也与风信子科和山茱萸科。虽然这类群体长期以来被认为不能令人满意，但没有令人信服的证据允许使用者选择一种界限而不是另一种界限; 现在有了。一般认为，唇形科和马鞭草科的界限必须重新划定，两者的内容也发生了较大变化，现在比以前更容易鉴别。因此，决定承认这些重新合并的家庭并不困难，如果不把它们分开，Lamiales 的大部分地区将会合并为一个家庭。这同样适用于杨柳科和茯苓科(Malpighiales) ，这两个以前很小的科已经接收了大部分古老的花科。在 Malpighiales 的一些地区，进化支系和限制税仍然很困难，但即使是这些支系的支持也在加强(Xi 等人，2012b)。大戟科植物已经出现了一些问题——在过去，人们可以很容易地识别大戟科植物，因为它们的果实爆裂，具有独特的持久柱。蒲兰科，一个相当不相关的分离，是相当不同的，由化学证据证实(存在硫代葡萄糖苷/芥子油) ，但有四个科组成了大戟科的大部分，仍然在同一部分的 Malpighiales 树(例如 Wurdack et al. 2004; Davis et al. 2005)。然而，没有任何分子证据证明这些大戟科分离种能够结合在一起，如果它们能够结合在一起，那么这部分树的分支表明以前没有认识到的新分类。因此，花生科似乎是嵌入在单一的排卵期大戟科(Davis 等人，2007年) ，并没有什么热情减少标志性的花生科为同义词。其姊妹支系为大戟科以外的生花科和众所周知的亚麻科。石竹目的核心关系，特别是在商陆科(可能有些令人惊讶)和墨尔本科(不那么令人惊讶)的关系是不完全理解和重新定义的分类单元的限制，随着关系变得越来越明显(见 Nyffeler & Eggli 2010; Christin 等人2011a; Brockington 等人2011; y. Yang 等人2015; Christenhusz 等人2014)。古老的凤眼兰科已经被打破了(特别是 Stull 等人2015年) ，然而，古老的 Olacaceae 的分支限制，主要是半寄生虫，仍然不清楚(Nickrent 等人2010年和参考文献)。

Many families in these pages are polythetic at the morphological level, that is, they lack unique features characterizing ("defining") all and only members of that family. They can be recognised phenetically only by the unique combinations of characters that they possess. This is the result of evolution; the synapomorphy characterizing a lineage may be lost or modified beyond easy recognition in some of its members, or the synapomorphy may appear to be identical to a feature that has evolved in parallel in quite unrelated plants. (Taxa in evolutionary classifications are also often polythetic.) Indeed, some families recognized here now include substantial variation as phenetically distinct derived groups are placed in their proper phylogenetic position - examples are the erstwhile Empetraceae, a wind-pollinated group, now included in Ericaceae, and the various derived, small-flowered aquatic and wind-pollinated groups that are included in the overwhelmingly large-flowered and animal-pollinated Plantaginaceae.

许多家庭在这些网页是多元的形态水平，也就是说，他们缺乏独特的特征(“定义”)所有和只有成员的家庭。它们只有通过它们所拥有的独特的字符组合才能被识别出来。这是进化的结果; 一个谱系的突触形态特征可能在其某些成员中丢失或改变得难以辨认，或者突触形态可能看起来与在相当不相关的植物中平行进化的特征相同。(在进化分类中的分类群通常也是多元的。)事实上，这里所确认的一些家族现在包括大量的变异，因为具有明显特征的衍生群体被放置在它们适当的系统发育位置，例如昔日的东洋扇贝族，一个风媒传粉的群体，现在包括在 Ericaceae，以及各种衍生的、小花的水生和风媒传粉的群体，包括在绝大多数大花和动物传粉的车前科。

In the past, problematic taxa tended to be assigned to groups using a few or even only a single character weighted particularly strongly on *a priori* grounds. The result was the recognition of conglomerate taxa such as Amentiferae (wind-pollinated), Rafflesiales (parasites), Nepenthales (carnivores), etc. (Cronquist 1981), all of which have been found be highly polyphyletic, and/or the segregation of families like the wind-pollinated Plantaginaceae s. str. (now much expanded) and Leitneriaceae (now in Simaroubaceae). Given the ever-increasing amount and complexity of morphological knowledge and the difficulty of carrying out complex multivariate analyses in one's head, a solution in the days before computers was to emphasize just one or a few characters thought to be evolutionarily important and delimit groups accordingly. Thus the Parietales included a number of families all of which had parietal placentation - and these families are now widely dispersed on the tree.

在过去，有问题的分类单元往往被分配到使用少数甚至只有一个字符加权特别强烈的先验理由的群体。结果表明，风媒植物 Amentiferae (风媒植物)、寄生植物 Rafflesiales (寄生植物)、食肉动物 Nepenthales (食肉动物)等砾岩分类群均具有高度的多门类性质，并且(或)出现了风媒植物车前科(Plantaginaceae) str。(现在大大扩展)和大叶菜科(现在在 Simaroubaceae)。由于形态学知识的数量和复杂性不断增加，而且人们很难在头脑中进行复杂的多变量分析，在计算机出现之前，一种解决方案就是强调一个或几个被认为具有进化重要性的字符，并据此划分群体。因此，Parietales 包括许多家庭，所有这些家庭都有顶叶胎座——这些家庭现在广泛分散在树上。

Indeed, we used to assume that features like highly scalariform vessel perforation plates or complete absence of vessels, or a flower with an androecium that had many stamens, a superior ovary, or separate petals, were necessarily "primitive", and conversely vessels with simple perforation plates, an androecium with few stamens, inferior ovary, or petals that were connnate were almost necessarily "advanced" (but c. f. Stebbins 1951). Such assumptions are incorrect (e.g. Soltis et al. 2005b); for the evolution of vessels in asterids, highly parallel/with reversals, see Lens et al. (2016). Carpels may become secondarily free; carpels may fail to close, the seeds then developing outside the confines of the carpel, as in some Aspagaraceae-Nolinoideae, Violaceae, Berberidaceae, Malvaceae-Sterculioideae, etc.; in *Peliosanthes teta*, perhaps the only species in *Peliosanthes* (Asparagaceae-Nolinoideae) the ovary varies from superior to inferior (Jessop 1976: species limits here need investigation!), as in Saxifragaceae, Apiales (esp. Pittosporaceae), Asterales (see Menyanthaceae), Poales, etc.; many-seeded carpels can evolve from few-seeded carpels (Razafimandimbison et al. 2008, but c.f. in part Beaulieu & Donoghue 2013); monoecy may be derived from dioecy (Schaefer & Renner 2010 and references) - and on it goes. Classic studies such as those by Babcock (e.g. 1947) on *Crepis* that assumed that evolution - in this case of the karyotype in particular - was unidirectional have needed comprehensive re-evaluation (Enke & Gemeinholzer 2008). Most if not all characters have reversed and/or evolved in parallel, even at the level of amino acid substitution, as in the independent acquisition of the phosphoenolpyruvate carboxylase (pepC) gene in C4 photosynthesis in grasses (Christin et al. 2007b; see also Bläsing et al. 2000; Anke et al. 2004; Reimann et al. 2004; Maia et al. 2012; Langel et al. 2010; Irmer et al. 2015; Fukushima et al. 2017; Later et al. 2018; etc.).

事实上，我们过去常常假设，高度鳞片状的导管穿孔板或者完全没有导管，或者雄蕊群有许多雄蕊、子房上位或者分开的花瓣等特征必然是“原始的”，相反，具有单穿孔板的导管，雄蕊群有少数雄蕊，子房下位或者合生的几乎必然是“先进的”(但是 c. f. Stebbins，1951年)。这种假设是不正确的(例如 Soltis 等人2005年 b) ; 关于星群、高度平行/有逆转的血管演变，见 Lens 等人(2016)。心皮可能第二次离生; 心皮可能无法闭合，种子在心皮之外发育，例如在一些防己科-念珠菌亚科、紫堇科、小檗科、锦葵科-梧桐亚科等; 在簇花球子草科，也许是唯一的天冬科(天冬科-念珠菌亚科)的种子从上到下不断变化(Jessop 1976: 物种界限需要调查!)例如 Saxifragaceae 的 Apiales (尤其是。多籽心皮可以从少籽心皮进化而来(razafimanddimbison 等，2008年，但是 c.f 部分 Beaulieu & Donoghue 2013年) ; 雌雄同株可能来源于雌雄异株(Schaefer & Renner，2010年及参考文献)-等等。诸如 Babcock (例如1947年)关于 Crepis 的经典研究假定进化——尤其是核型——是单向的，需要全面的重新评估(Enke & Gemeinholzer，2008年)。大多数(如果不是所有的)性状都发生了逆转和/或平行进化，甚至在氨基酸替代水平上也是如此，例如在禾草的光合作用中独立获得磷酸烯醇式丙酮酸羧化酶(pepC)基因(Christin 等人，2007年 b; 参见 Bläsing 等人，2000年; Anke 等人，2004年; Reimann 等人，2004年; Maia 等人，2012年; Langel 等人，2010年; Irmer 等人，2015年; 福岛等人，2017年; 后来等人，2018年等)。

Given the suggested relationships of some parasitic and aquatic groups, it can be very difficult to understand how they have evolved from their more morphologically conventional relatives, however, it may well be that our preconceptions as to likely or possible evolutionary change are at fault. With Podostemaceae sister to Hypericaceae, I look forward to seeing hypotheses to explain how the dramatic changes in the vegetative body that have made Podostemaceae so problematic for generations of systematists took place. That conventional wisdom has trouble in understanding or explaining how the morphologies of such groups can be related is largely a problem with conventional wisdom.

考虑到一些寄生生物和水生生物之间的关系，我们很难理解它们是如何从形态上更传统的近亲进化而来的，然而，很可能我们对可能或可能的进化变化的先入之见是错误的。作为广藿香科植物与金丝桃科植物的姐妹，我期待着看到假说来解释广藿香科植物体的戏剧性变化是如何让一代又一代的系统论者感到疑惑的。传统智慧在理解或解释这些群体的形态如何相关方面存在困难，这在很大程度上是传统智慧的问题。

Similar problems affect generic circumscriptions. Thus emphasising the importance of floral characters that reflect pollination syndromes when drawing generic boundaries has all too often led to taxa that are highly unsatisfactory phylogenetically (see e.g. Acanthaceae, Bignoniaceae, Campanulaceae, Ericaceae, Melastomataceae, Orchidaceae, etc.) while over-reliance on characters of fruit and seed (see particularly Brassicaceae and Apiaceae) has also led to questionable generic limits. Again, the more general problem has been caused by the use of one or a very few characters that have been weighted *a priori* to structure classifications (see also García et al. 2009). Working out limits for genera is rightly becoming a major preoccupation as some stability is now evident in higher level phylogenies and taxa. Here the discussions about changes to generic limits in the German flora - which of course have implications far beyond Germany - that have been assembled in Kadereit et al. (2016) make fascinating reading. Again, there are tensions between those who are happy with narrowly-drawn genera, other prefer their genera to be more broadly drawn; some of the changes have already been made, some are definitely needed, but remain to be carried out, and there are yet others where the basic phylogenetic evidence is still incomplete. In some cases piecemeal changes are being proposed based on a local perspective, while in others waiting for the bigger picture to materialize seems the sensible thing to do.

类似的问题也会影响通用界限。因此，在划分属间界限时强调反映授粉综合征的花部特征的重要性，往往导致极不理想的系统发育类群(如爵床科、大壬科、桔梗科、杜鹃科、野牡丹科、兰科等) ，而过分依赖果实和种子特征(特别是十字花科和伞形科)也导致了令人质疑的属间界限。同样，更普遍的问题是由于使用了一个或极少数字符，这些字符先验地被加权为结构分类(另见 García 等人，2009年)。因为在更高层次的系统发育和分类群中，一些稳定性是显而易见的，所以确定属的界限正成为当务之急。在这里，关于德国植物区系属性限制变化的讨论——当然其影响远远超出了德国——已经在 Kadereit 等人(2016)汇编成了引人入胜的阅读材料。同样，那些对狭隘的种属划分感到满意的人与其他人之间也存在紧张关系; 一些变化已经做出，一些肯定是需要的，但仍有待实施，还有一些基本的系统发育证据仍不完整。在某些情况下，零碎的改变是基于当地的视角提出的，而在另一些情况下，等待更大的图景实现似乎是明智的做法。

In conclusion. Some families as delimited here may not be easy to recognize, but remember that detecting relationships - use whatever characters you can, even if they are not obvious - and naming a plant - focus on obvious characters that may not reflect relationships - are quite different problems. Taxa, although "natural", may not be readily recognizable, indeed, it was in exactly this context that Lamarck described the basic principles of writing dichotomous keys in 1778. Of course, Lamarck's idea of nature was very different from ours - there was some kind of continuum of form between living organisms, with no major gaps anywhere - and this meant that his genera (for example) might well not be sharply distinct from each other. Perhaps the best way of identifying plants at the family level is by well-made multiple access keys, as in [Watson and Dallwitz](javascript:showImage('http://biodiversity.uno.edu/delta',600,500)) (1992a onwards: family limits there may differ substantially from those adopted here). Such keys free users from the constraints of dichotomous keys in which particular characters are needed at each step of the identification process before there can be further progress. Instead, whatever characters are evident on a specimen can be used in whatever order is convenient; when linked to illustrations, glossaries, etc., their power is enormous (see Dallwitz et al. 2000 [2006] for the principles underlying their construction and use). Nevertheless, dichotomous keys such as those of Hutchinson (1973), Franz Thonner (Geesink et al. 1981) and Cullen (2006) have their uses, although even in the last-named, despite its date of publication, the family limits accepted do not reflect much in the way of recent findings. Furthermore, as Mary Barkworth (pers. comm.) pointed out, the structuring of information in keys may mean that their users can acquire general knowledge about plants - although of course taxa coming out adjacent in keys may well not be at all related, a fact that is all too frequently forgotten. Identification aids are proliferating (e.g. Utteridge & Bramley 2014), but it is easy to make mistakes if you try to go too fast!

总而言之。这里的一些家庭可能不容易识别，但要记住，检测关系——尽可能使用任何角色，即使它们并不明显——和命名植物——侧重于可能不反映关系的明显角色——是完全不同的问题。塔克萨，虽然“自然”，可能不容易识别，事实上，正是在这种背景下，拉马克在1778年描述了编写二分法键的基本原则。当然，拉马克的自然观与我们的大不相同——生物体之间存在着某种连续的形式，没有任何重大的差异——这意味着他的属(例如)可能彼此之间没有明显的差异。也许在家庭一级鉴别植物的最佳方法是使用制作精良的多路钥匙，如 Watson 和 Dallwitz (1992a 以后: 那里的家庭限制可能与这里采用的大不相同)。这样的密钥使用户免于二分法密钥的约束，在识别过程的每个步骤中需要特定的字符，然后才能有进一步的进展。相反，一个标本上任何明显的字符都可以以任何方便的顺序使用; 当与插图、词汇表等联系在一起时，它们的力量是巨大的(参见 Dallwitz 等人2000[2006]中构建和使用这些字符的基本原则)。尽管如此，诸如 Hutchinson (1973) ，Franz Thonner (Geesink et al. 1981)和 Cullen (2006)的二分法检索也有它们的用途，尽管即使在最后一个命名中，尽管它的出版日期，被接受的家庭限制并没有以最近的发现的方式反映很多。此外，正如玛丽 · 巴克沃斯(演员)。委员会。)指出，密码匙中的资料结构可能意味着使用者可以获得有关植物的一般知识，尽管密码匙中相邻的分类群当然可能完全不相关，这个事实常常被人遗忘。识别辅助工具正在激增(例如，Utteridge & Bramley 2014) ，但是如果你试图走得太快，就很容易出错！

(When identifying large numbers of plants, even more efficient than either style of identification, and certainly lots more fun, is sight identification. However, unless one has a photographic memory, one has to build up a good general knowledge of comparative plant morphology, and it is on this the ability to make accurate identifications depends. When faced with an unknown plant, I always look for leaf teeth and stipules and dots of various kinds in the lamina and check leaf insertion; smelling crushed leaves can also be helpful. The short paragraphs added after most families may help in confirming familial identifications. In this context, nodal anatomy can usually be checked using a razor and a hand lens.)

(当识别大量植物时，比任何一种识别方式都更有效，当然更有趣的是视觉识别。然而，除非一个人拥有过目不忘的记忆力，否则他必须建立起一个关于比较植物形态学的良好的通识，而正是基于此，才有能力做出准确的识别。当面对一棵不知名的植物时，我总是在叶片上寻找叶齿、托叶和各种各样的点，并检查叶片插入情况; 闻碎叶子也有帮助。在大多数家庭之后添加的简短段落可能有助于确认家庭认同。在这种情况下，通常可以使用剃刀和手透镜检查结节的解剖结构

For the record, and for the little that it is worth, there are 4 orders and 13 families of gymnosperms characterised on these pages, and together they include some 82 genera and 947 species. For angiosperms, comparable figures are 57 orders, 446 families, 13,208 genera, and 261,750 species (of which monocots include 11 orders, 89 families, 2,759 genera and 52,760 species). Note, however, that higher mathematics was never my strong point, and anyway these are pretty meaningless figures; even for species, which some might concede smacked slightly more of reality than other taxa, estimates range as high as 422,000 (Govaerts 2001), and perhaps 10-20% more are currently undescribed (Joppa et al. 2010). Indeed, estimates of numbers of species in groups that one would have thought were well known vary widely, two examples being the daffodil genus, *Narcissus* (estimates in the last five years range from 15-81 species: Marques et al. 2017), and the bee orchid genus, *Ophrys* (16-252 species: e.g. Bateman et al. 2011a; Vereecken et al. 2011; Sedeek et al. 2014; Alibertis 2015: photographs!, see also [below](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asparagalesweb.htm#Orchidaceae)). Recent general estimates also highlight the issue: Christenhusz and Byng (2016) estimate that there are 295,383 species of flowering plants, while 369,434 species is the number in Nic Lughadha et al. (2016). Furthermore, Mallet (2013: p. 690) noted that "species counts over large areas of space and time [i.e., those in these pages!] represent only a sketchy measure of biodiversity, a measure that owes more to taxonomic and metphysical fashion than to science". Metaphysics aside, numbers of genera and species of course change daily. Nevertheless, as emphasized here, families are useful in teaching, we as a community can ensure that their limits remain largely stable, and by concentrating on relatively few of the larger families one can gain some familiarity with much of the world's flora. Generic names are even more used, and again, our goal should be to ensure stability in generic circumscriptions.

为了记录在案，也为了它的价值，有4个目和13科裸子植物的特点在这些网页上，他们包括大约82属和947种。被子植物的可比种数为57目446科13208属261750种(其中单子叶植物包括11目89科2759属52760种)。然而，请注意，高等数学从来不是我的强项，而且无论如何，这些都是相当没有意义的数字; 即使对于物种来说(有些物种可能承认比其他分类群稍微更接近现实) ，估计范围高达422,000(政府2001年) ，而且可能还有10-20% 的物种目前尚未被描述(约帕等人，2010年)。事实上，人们原本以为已经很熟悉的群体中的物种数量估计差别很大，其中两个例子是水仙属、水仙属(在过去五年中估计有15-81个物种: 马克斯等人2017年)和蜜蜂属、奥弗里斯(16-252个物种: 例如贝特曼等人2011年 a; 弗雷肯等人2011年; 塞迪克等人2014年; 阿里贝尔蒂斯2015年: 照片！，另见下文)。最近的一般估计也强调了这个问题: Christenhusz 和 Byng (2016年)估计被子植物有295,383种，而 Nic Lughadha 等人(2016年)估计有369,434种。此外，Mallet (2013: p. 690)指出，“物种计算在大面积的空间和时间[即，在这些页面! ]只是对生物多样性的粗略衡量，这种衡量更多地归功于分类学和元物理学的方式，而不是科学”。撇开形而上学不谈，种属的数量每天都在变化。然而，正如这里所强调的，家庭在教学中是有用的，我们作为一个社区可以确保他们的局限性在很大程度上保持稳定，通过集中在相对较少的较大的家庭中，人们可以对世界上的许多植物有所了解。泛型名称甚至被更多地使用，同样，我们的目标应该是确保泛型限制的稳定性。

**ON FORMING CLADE CHARACTERIZATIONS AND THINKING ABOUT APOMORPHIES**
[Back to Top](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/introductionnew.htm#top)

关于无共性的形成分支刻画与思考

The organization of the information throughout is hierarchical, that is, character states constant or almost constant in higher groupings are not mentioned at lower levels (see also Stevens et al. 2004b; Kellogg 2015). This is in line with a phylogeny- or tree-based system, yet it has, perhaps ironically, long been seen as being an advantage of many so-called natural systems, even those that owe nothing to evolutionary ideas (e.g. Cesalpino 1583; Jussieu 1789). However, there is much to do to make this style of presentation fully effective. In particular, whether character states more or less constant in a group are synapomorphies for it often waits for further clarification of relationships both within the group and between that group and its immediate relatives. For example, most Annonaceae have stamens with distinctive prolongations of the connective, but *Anaxagorea* is sister to the rest of the family and such connectives may not be a synapomorphy of Annonaceae, nor may indehiscent fruits and the absence of staminodes (e.g. Scharaschkin & Doyle 2005, 2006). As more is found out about phylogenies, such examples multiply, so the dismemberment of the Icacinaceae s.l. (Stull et al. 2015) has meant that the characterisation of the large [euasterid](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/icacinalesweb.html#euasterids) clade has been clarified, which has important implications when we think about euasterid diversification.

整个信息的组织是分层的，也就是说，较高级别的字符状态不变或几乎不变在较低级别没有提到(另见 Stevens 等人2004b; Kellogg 2015)。这符合系统发生学或树基系统，然而，也许具有讽刺意味的是，它长期以来一直被视为许多所谓的自然系统的优势，即使是那些没有进化思想的系统(例如: Cesalpino 1583; Jussieu 1789)。然而，要使这种风格的演示充分有效，还有很多工作要做。特别是，无论性格状态在一个群体中或多或少是不变的，都是突触遗传学，因为它经常等待群体内部以及群体与其直系亲属之间关系的进一步澄清。例如，大多数番荔枝科植物的雄蕊具有明显的结缔组织延长，但 Anaxagorea 是其他家族的姐妹，这种连接体可能不是番荔枝科植物的突触形态，也不可能是不开裂的果实和缺少雄蕊(例如 Scharaschkin & Doyle 2005,2006)。随着更多关于系统进化的发现，这样的例子越来越多，所以 Icacinaceae s.l. 的分裂意味着大型真角色塑造科的分支已经被澄清，这对我们思考真亚目的多样化有着重要的意义。

The character hierarchy was built up by first drawing up lengthy descriptions of families and then fitting the characters in the descriptions to molecular-based trees with rather conservative topologies. Many of the states of some characters at the base of the angiosperm tree are fairly obvious, hence the fairly lengthy characterisation (apomorphies and plesiomorphies definitely mixed!) for the angiosperms as a whole (but c.f. Sauquet et al. 2017). For some characters, I have worked up the tree, placing them as high as the evidence suggested. Otherwise, features in common to each clade, whether order, families within an order, or groups of orders, are those that are as far as is known common to all the family characterizations in that clade; they may also be synapomorphies (but see below), and are placed at the lowest level in the tree for which there is information available. For some features I have used both approaches, but confusion should be minimal. As relationships and our knowledge of the variation within characters improve, the top-down and bottom-up approaches will merge.

字符层次是建立起来的，首先起草冗长的描述家族，然后拟合字符的描述，以分子为基础的树与相当保守的拓扑。被子植物树基部的一些人物的许多状态是相当明显的，因此相当长的角色塑造是相当长的被子植物作为一个整体(但是 c.f. 索奎特等人2017)。对于一些角色，我已经在树上画好了，把他们放在证据所显示的高度。否则，每个分支的共同特征，无论是顺序、一个顺序中的家族还是一组顺序，都是那些已知的该分支中所有家族特征的共同特征; 它们也可能是突触遗传(但见下文) ，并放置在有可用信息的树的最低级别。对于某些特性，我同时使用了这两种方法，但是混淆应该是最小的。随着关系和我们对字符内部变化的了解的提高，自上而下和自下而上的方法将会合并。

Trees based on morphology alone often have little support, and they may silently lead the user astray (e.g. Zhang et al. 1992). Nevertheless, the validity of an approach that fits morphological variation to a molecular tree may be questioned (but see e.g. Doyle & Endress 2011 and earlier papers). However, I think it rather unlikely that branches that are well supported in molecular analyses will be overturned by morphological data. Analysis of morphological data alone provides support for many of the clades evident in molecule-only analyses, and in conjunction with molecular data may lead to increased support for clades (e.g. Hufford 1992; Nandi et al. 1998: here adding morphological data reduces support for a number of critical clades, too, a not-uncommon phenomenon; Doyle & Endress 2000), however, in none of these papers is the use of morphology without ambiguity. Thus I have been wary of putting much weight on clades that have only morphological support, but molecule-based clades with low bootstrap or jacknife values support values (esp. below 70%) or posterior probabilies (below 0.95) are also treated sceptically - indeed, that we still rely so much on variation in the chloroplast genome alone to construct phylogenies is worrisome, although things are changing. Other reasons for prefering to fit morphological variation to a tree are mentioned below.

仅仅基于形态学的树常常没有什么支持，它们可能会默默地将用户引入歧途(例如 Zhang 等人1992)。然而，符合分子树形态变异的方法的有效性可能会受到质疑(但是参见 Doyle & Endress 2011和更早的论文)。然而，我认为在分子分析中得到很好支持的分支不太可能被形态学数据颠覆。形态学数据本身的分析为许多分子分析中明显的分支提供了支持，并与分子数据结合可能导致对分支的支持增加(例如 Hufford 1992; Nandi 等人1998: 在这里添加形态学数据也减少了对一些关键分支的支持，这是一个不少见的现象; Doyle & Endress 2000) ，然而，在这些论文中没有一篇是使用形态学没有歧义。因此，我一直小心翼翼地把过多的重量放在只有形态学支持，但分子为基础的分支低自举值或 jacknife 值支持值(尤其是。低于70%)或后部概率(低于0.95)也受到怀疑——事实上，我们仍然如此依赖叶绿体基因组的变异来构建系统发育是令人担忧的，尽管情况正在发生变化。其他的原因，喜欢适合树形态变异在下面提到。

Morphological and molecular data are very rarely in irreconcilably strong conflict. However, examples that tend in that direction are the relative positions of the Monimiaceae and Hernandiaceae (Laurales), and there have also been arguments about the position of Hanguanaceae (Commelinales [see below; now very likely] or Zingiberales?), and of *Triplostegia* (is it in Caprifoliaceae-Dipsacacoideae or -Valerianoideae? - see [Dipsacoideae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/dipsacalesweb.htm#Dipsacaceae)). Although trees based on analyses of morphological data alone rarely command much support, Weins et al. (2010 and references) is an example of the integration of morphological and molecular data, and of fossils and extant organisms.

形态学数据和分子数据极少发生不可调和的强烈冲突。然而，向这个方向发展的例子是 Monimiaceae 和 hernandez aceae (樟科)的相对位置，还有关于 Hanguanaceae (鸭跖目[见下文; 现在很可能]或者姜目?)的位置的争论)和三倍体植物(属于忍冬科-续断亚科还是-缬草亚科？- 参阅川续断亚科)。虽然仅仅基于形态学数据分析的树很少得到很多支持，但是 Weins 等人(2010年和参考文献)是形态学和分子数据、化石和现存生物体的整合的一个例子。

Indeed, the general congruence between morphological and molecular data is impressive and heartening, and many clades can be characterised morphologically. It seemed in 1998 that there were no unambiguous morphological synapomorphies for angiosperm orders (K. Bremer 2000), and this is still true if by "unambiguous" is meant "non-homoplasious". However, many orders can be characterised and have synapomorphies (see below), even if these are homoplasious and morphologically indistinguishable (at least at the current level of morphological and developmental observation) from synapomorphies elsewhere on the tree.

实际上，形态学和分子学数据之间的一致性是令人印象深刻和振奋人心的，许多分支可以在形态学上进行特征描述。似乎在1998年，没有明确的形态联会遗传学被子植物目(k. Bremer 2000) ，这仍然是正确的，如果“明确的”是指“非同质性”。然而，许多序列可以特征化并具有突触共同性(见下文) ，即使这些与树上其他地方的突触共同性和形态上难以区分(至少在目前形态学和发育观察水平上)。

Identifying apomorphies is important because understanding the evolution of characters is one of our major goals. For this, several preconditions must be met. One needs to have an accurate, robust phylogeny, one has to have examined the right taxa both from the point of view of morphology and molecules, one has to have coded the characters correctly (i.e., delimited states appropriately), one has to have used the right model of evolution when fitting the variation to the tree, and finally, and little discussed here (but see e.g. the notes on the [diversification and evolution of angiosperms](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/amborellalesweb2.htm#Evolution)), one has to establish the right temporal context and to factor in other relevant aspects of the environment (see e.g. Omland 1999; Stevens 2006b).

识别非营利性是重要的，因为理解字符的演变是我们的主要目标之一。为此，必须满足几个前提条件。一个人需要有一个准确、健全的系统发育，一个人必须从形态学和分子学的角度检查正确的分类群，一个人必须正确地编码字符(即，适当地分隔状态) ，一个人必须使用正确的进化模式来适应树的变化，最后，在这里很少讨论(但是看看被子植物的多样化和进化的笔记) ，一个人必须建立正确的时间上下文，并考虑到环境的其他相关方面(例如: Omland 1999; Stevens 2006b)。

On each order page the features associated with each node leading to the order in question are summarised, and putative synapomorphies for the order, families, etc., will be found in the page itself (I began to indicate synapomorphies only in xii.2011), although it is clear that one has to be very cautious when talking about character evolution. If the synapomorphies here are compared with those in particular studies cited (e.g. Turgeon et al. 2001; Bremer et al. 2001; Endress 2001; Albach et al. 2001a; Judd et al. 2003; Judd & Olmstead 2004; D. Soltis et al. 2005b; Zhang et al. 2006), differences may be found. Although such studies have been integrated into the characterisations as far as possible, there are several reasons why there may be these differences.

在每个订单页面上，与每个节点相关的特征导致问题的顺序被总结，并假定的突触营养模式为顺序，家族等，将在页面本身中找到(我开始指出突触营养模式只在 xii. 2011) ，虽然很明显，人们在谈论性格演变时必须非常谨慎。如果将这里的突触遗传与那些引用的特定研究进行比较(例如特金等人2001年; 布雷默等人2001年; Endress 2001年; Albach 等人2001年; Judd 等人2003年; Judd & Olmstead 2004年; d. Soltis 等人2005年 b; Zhang 等人2006年) ，可能会发现差异。尽管这些研究已经尽可能地被纳入特征之中，但是可能存在这些差异的原因有几个。

**- Firstly**, I may not have found all the information about a particular character, there may be disagreement over its interpretation (e.g. Austrobaileyales), or I have added unpublished information (e.g. Primulaceae and their relatives, nodal anatomy, etc.; Diapensiaceae, leaf ptyxis; and Peridiscaceae, Centroplacaceae, etc.).

- 首先，我可能没有找到关于某一特征的所有资料，可能对其解释有不同的意见(例如木兰藤目) ，或者我添加了未发表的资料(例如报春花科及其近缘植物、节的解剖结构等; 大刺藓科、叶的习性; 以及百合科、山苍子科等)。

**- Secondly**, the sampling of nearly all molecular studies is incomplete, although it is fast improving. Unfortunately, the sampling of the morphological and chemical characters the evolution of which we are interested in understanding is also often very poor, yet it is not improving fast. For many anatomical, chemical and embryological characters that are confidently said to characterise families and other groups, we all too often have no idea if those characters are applicable to the whole clade, or just to a subgroup within that clade. Thus Albach et al. (2001a, see also D. Soltis et al. 2005b) assign possession of iridoids to the base of the asterid I + II clades. However, this feature is placed higher up the tree here, partly because of topological uncertainties, but partly because in [Lamiales](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/lamialesweb.htm#Lamiales) (for example), the first four clades that are successively sister to the remaining Lamiales either lack iridoids or (most Oleaceae) have iridoids different from those found in the other members of the clade. Similar problems arise when thinking of the evolution of ellagic acid in [Ericales](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/ericalesweb.htm#Ericales) (Stevens 2006b). Indeed, Much older literature, especially that from ca 1870-1920, remains invaluable, since it includes surveys, often never improved on since, of various aspects of plant anatomy and morphology for particular groups.

其次，几乎所有分子研究的抽样都不完整，尽管它正在迅速改善。不幸的是，我们感兴趣的形态学和化学性状的进化取样往往也很贫乏，然而它并没有得到很快的改善。对于许多解剖学、化学和胚胎学的特征，我们常常不知道这些特征是否适用于整个分支，或者仅仅适用于该分支中的一个亚群。因此 Albach 等人(2001年 a，也见 d. Soltis 等人2005年 b)将环烯醚萜归属于星号 i + II 分支的基部。然而，这个特征被放置在树的更高处，部分是因为地形的不确定性，但是部分是因为在 Lamiales (例如) ，前四个相继姐妹于剩余的 Lamiales 要么缺乏环烯醚萜要么(大多数木犀科)有环烯醚萜不同于在其他支系成员中发现的。当我们思考 Ericales 鞣花酸的演变时，同样的问题也出现了(Stevens 2006b)。事实上，许多较早的文献，特别是1870-1920年的文献，仍然是无价的，因为它包括了对特定种群的植物解剖学和形态学的各个方面的调查，往往从未改进过。

**- Thirdly**, there are then the small matters of character state delimitation and ancestral state reconstruction/character optimisation...

- 第三，还有一些小问题，如特征状态划分和祖先状态重建/特征优化..。

Here there are some general issues to think about first. Sattler (e.g. 1992) has long insisted that our thoughts as it were get trapped inside the terms we use, while Rutishauser and Sattler (1985), Kirchoff et al. (2008), and others outline different ways of thinking about morphology. Here the approach advocated i.a. by Prusinkiewicz and Barbier de Reuille (2010) as they think about plant form - the result of the activity of self-organizing proceses of the plant rather than being under immediate genetic control - very helpful as an antidote; throw in processes like heterochrony and heterotopy (e.g. Baum & Donoghue 2002), and our appreciation of morphology can change dramatically. Mathews and Kramer (2012) also help us to think about evolution of form and how novelties might develop over the course of evolutionary history. The most important thing to remember when using botanical terms is that just because some aspect of an organism is dignified by a sesquipedalian word, this by no means signifies that the term refers to an interesting part of "reality" (see also Kirchoff et al. 2008 and references). As Hesse et al. (2009b: p. 27) noted when writing about pollen morphology "Nature itself neither needs categories nor has any knowledge of them" and "categories are artificial and always delimited by an individual or collective convention". Humans make and define botanical terms, and we use them to facilitate communication, although all too often we take them to be "real" - and then they can be as much an impediment to our understanding as anything else. The terms we use, whether in palynology to describe the shape or surface of pollen grains (e.g. Punt et al. 2006; Hesse et al. 2009b), or in general morphology to describe leaf shape (e.g. see Stearn 1992), may well function quite effectively in communication/description while at the same time being inappropriate for use in character optimization - indeed, the caveats in Hesse et al. (2009b), with sections headed "Inherence of Misrepresentation" and "Controversial or Fuzzy Terms", should make one pause for thought.

这里有一些需要首先考虑的一般性问题。Sattler (举例来说，1992年)一直坚持认为我们的思想被困在我们所使用的术语中，而 Rutishauser 和 Sattler (1985年) ，Kirchoff 等人(2008年) ，以及其他人概述了关于形态学的不同思维方式。在这里，Prusinkiewicz 和 Barbier de Reuille (2010)所倡导的方法，因为他们认为植物的形态——植物自组织过程活动的结果，而不是在即时的遗传控制下——作为一种解毒剂，非常有用; 加上异染和异位等过程(例如，异染和多诺霍2002) ，我们对形态的欣赏可以发生巨大变化。Mathews 和 Kramer (2012)也帮助我们思考形态的进化，以及在进化史的过程中新奇事物可能如何发展。在使用植物学术语时，最重要的是要记住，仅仅因为一个生物体的某些方面是由一个同音异义词构成的，这绝不意味着这个术语指的是“现实”中有趣的部分(参见 Kirchoff 等人2008年的文献)。正如 Hesse 等人(2009年 b: 第27页)在撰写花粉形态学时所指出的,”自然本身不需要分类，也不需要对它们有任何认识”,”分类是人为的，总是由个体或集体习俗划定的”。人类创造和定义植物学术语，我们使用它们来促进交流，尽管我们常常把它们当作“真实的”——然后它们可能像其他任何东西一样阻碍我们的理解。我们使用的术语，无论是在孢粉学中描述花粉粒的形状或表面(例如 Punt et al. 2006; Hesse et al. 2009b) ，还是在一般形态学中描述叶子形状(例如 Stearn 1992) ，可能在交流/描述中非常有效，同时不适合用于字符优化——实际上，Hesse 等(2009b)的告诫，带有标题为“不正当手法引诱的继承”和“有争议或模糊的术语”的章节，应该让人停下来思考。

The choice of characters and delimititation of their states is a first step to take as we attempt to flesh out phylogenies. For a still useful introduction to the general issue of characters and what they might signify, see the essays in Wagner (2001), and for different ways of thinking about characters, see Kirchoff et al. (2008). Characters and their states ("anthers" and "introrse"/"extrorse"/"latrorse") as they are generally used come from a careful study of morphology, with similar structures on different organisms being compared. Here Remane's three main criteria of "homology"/similarity, special properties, position, and intermediates, are very useful (see Remane 1952; Kaplan 1997: 1 ch. 1; c.f. Endress 2011c, p. 122 - "too limited"), as also when aligning DNA sequences; for how to relate genotype and phenotype using the concept of persistent homology, a somewhat related issue, see e.g. M. Li et al. (2018 and references) and Larson (2018). However, Remane's criteria may not yield an unambiguous answer as to what a structure "is", even given a solid phylogeny to provide context for the subsequent interpretation of the structure in question. As Endress (2005c) observed, a number of features - position, function, development, shape, anatomy, histology, gene activity, and relationships to other taxa that clearly have petals - can be used to distinguish a petal (for example) from other floral structures. And if a petal lacks one of these points of similarity, is it thereby not a petal?, or if it has just one, is it a petal? So what about the outer members of the perianth of *Nymphaea* which may be part green and part coloured on the outside (Warner et al. 2009)?

选择字符和划分它们的状态是我们尝试充实系统发育的第一步。关于角色的一般问题以及它们可能意味着什么仍然有用的介绍，请参阅瓦格纳(2001年)的散文，以及对角色的不同思考方式，请参阅 Kirchoff 等人(2008年)。通常使用的字符及其状态(“花药”和“内向”/“外向”/“ latrorse”)来自对形态学的仔细研究，并比较了不同生物体上的相似结构。这里 Remane 关于“同源”/相似性、特殊性质、位置和中间体的三个主要标准非常有用(见 Remane 1952; Kaplan 1997:1 ch。1; c.f. Endress 2011c，p. 122-“ too limited”) ，以及在对齐 DNA 序列时; 关于如何使用持久同源性的概念来关联基因型和表型，一个有点相关的问题，见 m. Li 等人(2018年和参考文献)和 Larson (2018年)。然而，Remane 的标准可能不会给出一个明确的答案，即什么是一个结构“是”，甚至给一个坚实的系统发展史，以提供上下文的解释结构的问题。正如 Endress (2005年 c)所观察到的，一些特征——位置、功能、发育、形状、解剖学、组织学、基因活性，以及与其他明显有花瓣的分类群的关系——可以用来区分花瓣(例如)与其他花结构。如果一片花瓣缺少这些相似点中的一个，那么它不就是一片花瓣吗？或者如果只有一个花瓣，那它是一个花瓣吗？那么，Nymphaea 花被的外部成员可能部分是绿色，部分是有色的(Warner et al. 2009) ？

At the genetic level the situation is equally complex. Genes do not necessarily "do" particular things, rather, expression may be a continuous variable. The expression of one gene can be affected by the expression of others, genes are parts of networks, and can be co-opted to act in a variety of different contexts. Thus Maturen et al. (2005) found that floral organ genes (B- and C-class) were expressed in the large, white inflorescence bracts of *Cornus* (see also Costa et al. 2005), while A-class genes can be expressed in the inflorescence, or even in leaves (Prenner et al. 2011: *Euphorbia* and Asteraceae). In the inverted repeat loss clade (Fabaceae-Faboideae) *FLO*/*LFY* genes, normally floral meristem identity genes, are also expressed in the leaves - which have subtly different morphologies than those of other Fabaceae (Champagne et al. 2007; Wang et al. 2008; Peng et al. 2011; Townsley & Sinha 2012). In *Solanum* there are similarities at the genetic level between shoot branching and leaf dissection, and development of the abscission zone of the fruit, made up of arrested meristematic cells, is also involved in this regulatory network (Busch et al. 2011; Périlleux et al. 2014).

在基因水平上，情况同样复杂。基因不一定“做”特定的事情，相反，表达可能是一个连续变量。一个基因的表达可以受到其他基因的表达的影响，基因是网络的一部分，并且可以在不同的情况下被选择作用。因此 Maturen 等人(2005年)发现花器官基因(b-和 c 类)在山茱萸的大型白色花序苞片中表达(见 Costa 等人2005年) ，而 a 类基因可以在花序中表达，甚至在叶片中也可以表达(Prenner 等人2011年: 大戟属和菊科)。在反向重复缺失(Fabaceae-Faboideae) FLO/LFY 基因中，通常的花分生组织特性基因也在叶片中表达——这些基因的形态与其他 Fabaceae 基因略有不同(Champagne et al. 2007; Wang et al. 2008; Peng et al. 2011; Townsley & Sinha 2012)。茄属植物的分枝和叶片解剖在遗传水平上有相似之处，果实的脱落区的发育也参与了这一调控网络(Busch 等人，2011年; Périlleux 等人，2014年)。

I have thought a bit about the delimitation of characters and their states (Stevens 2000 for literature), but not nearly enough. One serious problem is that we commonly describe the variation we see, whether in plant architecture, leaf venation, pollen, ovule, nucellus, endosperm, embryo and many other organ systems, as "types" - the solanad type of embryogenesis, *Allium* type of embryo sac, etc.. Such terms often represent the categorization of simultaneous variation of many features, but these features often vary more or less continuously, and/or are complex, and/or the various elements that make them up may vary independently; all this variation effectively gets "lost" when we use these terms. But worse, we tend to think that evolution is a matter of one "type" of endosperm development (for example) evolving into another. Even when looking at what we think is a single character, we often find that its states refer to a part of a continuum of variation of that character such as [character] ovule curvature, [states] ovule anatropous vs campylotropous vs ... (and anther opening mentioned above). Many of these states have been used in the botanical literature for well over a century, but all too often they are the result of the more or less arbitrary division of a continuum of variation (see Gift & Stevens 1997 for how this works in practice), as with ovule curvature itself. Although such character states may seem to communicate "information", whether they are necessarily suitable for either phylogenetic analysis or understanding evolution (see Linder & Bouchenak-Khelladi 2017) is decidedly questionable. Thus when interpreting the literature (e.g. Stevens 2000, 2006b) - and this site, too - one should bear such problems in mind. Of course, as character states change, so may our ideas of evolution (e.g. Lamb Frye & Kron 2003; Hibbett 2004), and Tomescu and Groover (2018) provide a nice example of this as they decompose "vascular cambium" into its underlying variables and then think about the evolution of cambium - or, rather, these variables - across all vascular plants.

我想了一点关于人物和他们的状态的界限(史蒂文斯2000文学) ，但是远远不够。一个严重的问题是，我们通常把我们看到的变异，无论是在植物结构，叶脉，花粉，胚珠，珠心，胚乳，胚胎和许多其他器官系统，描述为“类型”——茄子型胚胎发生，葱型胚囊等。这些术语通常表示许多特征同时变化的分类，但这些特征通常或多或少地连续变化，而且/或者很复杂，而且/或者组成这些特征的各种元素可能各自不同; 当我们使用这些术语时，所有这些变化实际上都”丢失”了。但更糟糕的是，我们倾向于认为进化是一种胚乳发育的“类型”(例如)进化成另一种。甚至当我们观察我们认为是单一性状的时候，我们经常发现它的状态指的是该性状连续变化的一部分，例如[性状]胚珠弯曲，[状态]胚珠倒生与斜生与... ... (以及上面提到的花药开放)。这些状态中的许多已经在植物学文献中使用了一个多世纪，但是它们常常是或多或少地随意划分连续变化的结果(见 Gift & Stevens 1997年关于实践中这是如何工作的) ，就像胚珠弯曲本身一样。尽管这些特征状态似乎是在交流“信息”，但它们是否必然适用于系统发育分析或理解进化论(参见 Linder & Bouchenak-Khelladi 2017)是绝对值得怀疑的。因此，当解释文献(例如，史蒂文斯2000,2006b)-和这个网站，也-人们应该记住这些问题。当然，随着性格状态的改变，我们的进化观念也可能改变(例如 Lamb Frye & Kron 2003; Hibbett 2004) ，以及 Tomescu 和 Groover (2018)提供了一个很好的例子，因为他们将“形成层”分解为其基本变量，然后考虑形成层——或者更确切地说，这些变量——在所有维管植物中的进化。

Furthermore, understanding even current literature can be difficult because the terms that we use often have no fixed definitions - the term "panicle" can be understood only if you know how the author of the publication in which you find the term was using it (see also Endress 2010b). As Rickett (1954: 2, emphasis in original) noted, "To be uncertain whether "glabrous" means "free from hairs *and* roughness" or only "free from hairs" is as bad as if π [pi] should stand sometimes for the ratio of a circle to its diameter and sometimes for something else; or as if Cu meant sometimes "copper" and sometimes "brass". Yet this is the state of affairs in botany today". Well over a half century later, this is still the state of affairs. In this context, an ontology that is generally accepted by botanists is essential (see also Vogt et al. 2010); the [Plant Ontology Consortium](http://archive.plantontology.org) is a resource here, but see Kirchoff et al. (2008) for caveats.

此外，即使是理解当前的文献也可能很困难，因为我们使用的术语往往没有固定的定义——只有当你知道出版物的作者是如何使用这个术语的时候，才能理解”圆锥”这个术语(另见 Endress 2010b)。正如 Rickett (1954:2，原文强调)所指出的,”不确定”无毛”是指”没有毛发和粗糙度”，还是仅仅”没有毛发”，就好像 π [ pi ]有时代表圆与其直径的比率，有时代表其他东西; 或者好像 Cu 有时代表”铜”，有时代表”黄铜”。然而，这就是今天植物学的现状”。半个多世纪过去了，现在的情况依然如此。在这种情况下，一个被植物学家普遍接受的本体论是必不可少的(参见 Vogt 等人2010) ; 植物本体论联盟是这里的一个资源，但是请参见 Kirchoff 等人(2008)的说明。

The delimitation of states and characters does not necessarily become easier with increasing knowledge. Thus Buzgo et al. (2004) and Matthews and Endress (2005) show how hard it can be to distinguish between e.g. prophylls and other floral structures, while Penet et al. (2005) find that not all monosulcate pollen in monocots has the same developmental pathway, and suggest that therefore such pollen may not have the same ancestral state. There are all intermediates between vessels and tracheids (Schneider & Carlquist 2009; Carlquist & Schneider 2010; Carlquist 2012a), between fully superior and fully inferior ovaries (Soltis & Hufford 2002), floral phyllotaxis may be very labile, especially in magnoliids and members of the ANITA grade (Staedler & Endress 2009), leaves are not always easily distinguishable from other structures (Rutishauser 1999) - and on it goes. But this is in part a level or universe issue. As a comparison increases in extent, what one thought were differences between structures may disappear - and whether this is important, interesting or simply irrelevant will depend on the problem at hand.

随着知识的增加，状态和字符的划分并不一定变得容易。因此，Buzgo 等人(2004年)和 Matthews and Endress (2005年)展示了区分预先叶和其他花结构是多么困难，而 Penet 等人(2005年)发现单子叶植物中的单槽花粉并非都有相同的发育途径，因此这种花粉可能不具有相同的祖先状态。在导管和管胞之间都有中间层(Schneider & Carlquist，2009; Carlquist & Schneider，2010; Carlquist，2012a) ，在完全上位和完全下位的子房之间(Soltis & Hufford，2002) ，花叶状花序可能非常柔软，特别是在木兰属植物和 ANITA 等级的成员中(Staedler & Endress，2009) ，叶子并不总是很容易与其他结构区分(Rutishauser，1999)。但这在某种程度上是一个层面或宇宙问题。随着比较程度的增加，人们所认为的结构之间的差异可能会消失——这是重要的、有趣的还是完全不相关的，将取决于手头的问题。

For these and other reasons, character states, the 0's and 1's of a morphological data matrix, are all too often some degrees removed from the actual structures observed on individual specimens, furthermore, all too often there is no clear link between these states and specimens/species on which the structures were observed. Specimens are prepared, observations/measurements made, and these somehow become converted to statements about species and then of more inclusive groups (Stevens 1996). Even for this site, it would be have been ideal if observations and literature could have been directly linked at the level of individual species and specimens in a database - this was obvious even as the possibility of APweb was being discussed in the late 1990s. This would allow problems like wrongly assigned taxa to be dealt with easily - remove a taxon from a family, and all information linked to that taxon would be removed at the same time, perfect when dealing with developing phylogenies. Fortunately, this is an area where are major changes underway, changes spurred by the advent of molecular data and what very soon became a mandatory requirement for DNA sequences used in publications to be deposited in the publicly accessible databases like [GenBank](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/genbank/) (founded in 1982) - publication depends on sequences being made available. Resources like the [Dryad Digital Repository](http://www.datadryad.org) (it started in 2008) make the various kinds of data that underpin systematic/evolutionary publications accessible. However, as Drew et al. (2013) noted, alignments and trees were very often not deposited, despite encouragements to do so, and this has made earlier studies of less value than they might have been. There has been nothing that has been functioning as a Genbank for morphological data, and it is often impossible to evaluate whether states in a particular study have been delimited satisfactorily; as in much of taxonomy as a whole there are few data in the sense of observations that can be linked to specimens and that can be reanalyzed when necessary. Data matrices can be deposited in places like [MorphoBank](https://morphobank.org/) (O'Leary & Kaufman 2011), and, more generally, in Dryad, and so you can, for example, access the matrix used by Sauquet et al. (2017) in their work on the ancestral angiosperm flower. More extensive data matrices are being developed (e.g. Sauquet 2016: [PROTEUS](http://eflower.myspecies.info/proteus), not yet open access); Sauquet and Magallón (2018) rightly emphasize the importance of a standardized, fully documented open-access database for plant morphology. Ultimately, fitting basic variation such as measurements, not character states, to a tree allows considerable flexibility in understanding morphology in the context of local phylogenies (see also Stevens 2000; Endress 2005c, but c.f. Weins et al. 2010 for problems here), and this approach has also been used at higher levels, as in a study looking at the evolution of pollen size and shape in Myrtales (Kriebel et al. 2017; see also Parins-Fukuchi 2017).

由于这些和其他原因，特征状态，0和1的形态学数据矩阵，往往是从实际结构上观察到的个别标本，而且往往没有明确的联系，这些状态和标本/物种之间的结构被观察到。标本是准备好的，观察/测量是做好的，并且这些以某种方式转化为关于物种的陈述，然后是更具包容性的群体(Stevens 1996)。即使对这个网站来说，如果观察和文献能够在数据库中的个别物种和标本一级直接联系起来，那将是理想的——即使在1990年代后期讨论 APweb 的可能性时，这一点也是显而易见的。这将使错误分配的分类群之类的问题可以很容易地处理——从一个家族中移除一个分类群，并且所有与该分类群相关的信息将同时被移除，在处理发展中的分类系统时非常完美。幸运的是，这是一个正在发生重大变化的领域，分子数据的出现带来了变化，很快出版物中使用的 DNA 序列必须存入诸如基因银行(1982年成立)之类的公开数据库——出版取决于序列是否可以获得。像 Dryad 数字图书馆(创建于2008年)这样的资源使得支撑系统/进化出版物的各种数据都可以访问。然而，正如德鲁等人(2013年)指出的那样，尽管人们鼓励这样做，但是排列和树木经常没有被保存，这使得早期的研究没有那么有价值。在形态学数据方面，没有什么东西像 Genbank 一样发挥作用，而且通常不可能评估某一特定研究中的状态是否已经满意地划分出来; 就像许多分类学整体而言，很少有观察数据可以与标本联系起来，并且在必要时可以重新分析。数据矩阵可以存放在像 MorphoBank (o’leary & Kaufman，2011)这样的地方，更广泛地说，存放在 Dryad 中，因此，你可以，例如，访问 Sauquet 等人(2017)在他们研究被子植物祖先花的工作中使用的矩阵。更广泛的数据矩阵正在开发中(例如，Sauquet 2016: PROTEUS，尚未开放存取) ; Sauquet 和 magallon (2018)正确地强调了标准化的、完全文档化的开放存取数据库对植物形态学的重要性。最终，将基本的变异，比如测量值，而不是特征状态，拟合到一棵树上，可以在当地系统发育的背景下，获得相当大的灵活性来理解形态学(参见 Stevens 2000; Endress 2005 c，但 c.f. Weins 等人2010的问题在这里) ，这种方法也已经在更高层次上得到应用，比如在一项关于 Myrtales 花粉大小和形状进化的研究中(Kriebel 等人2017; 参见 Parins-Fukuchi 2017)。

A good example of the kinds of problems faced are in the description of endosperm morphology and an understanding of its evolution, particularly in monocots. Tobe and Kadokawa (2010) discuss endosperm morphology in terms of cellular and helobial types (Stenar 1925 for early literature; Swamy & Parameswaran 1962). However, this distinction, commonly employed in the literature, does not capture the subtleties of endosperm development (see especially Floyd et al. 1999; Floyd & Friedman 2000, 2001 for alternatives; Rudall et al. 2009b). The initial division of the endosperm is highly asymmetric in Araceae, with subsequent cell divisions initially occurring only in the micropylar chamber; the family is considered to have cellular endosperm (Tobe & Kadokawa 2010; see also Maheshwari & Khanna 1957). The chalazal cells here are sometimes massive (e.g. Paremeswaran 1959). Initial asymmetry in endosperm development characterizes helobial endosperm development, so Araceae could also be characterized as having a form of helobial endosperm; Acoraceae also show similar asymmetry (Buell 1938). There is also variation in whether the micropylar (e.g. Nymphaeales) or both micropylar and chalazal (*Amborella*: most from the latter) domains give rise to the bulk of the endosperm. The evolutionary history of nuclear endosperm development is also unclear (Olsen 2004; see e.g. Zou et al. 2001 for subtleties in its development), and there is variation in e.g. nuclear endosperm development, as within Poaceae (Leroux et al. 2014). For further discussion about helobial endosperm, see e.g. Kaplan (1981).

胚乳形态的描述和对胚乳形态演化的理解，尤其是单子叶植物的胚乳形态演化，就是一个很好的例子。Tobe 和 Kadokawa (2010年)讨论胚乳形态的细胞和细胞类型(早期文献 Stenar 1925; Swamy & Parameswaran 1962)。然而，这种区别，在文献中普遍使用，并没有捕捉胚乳发育的微妙之处(特别是 Floyd 等人1999; Floyd & Friedman 2000,2001 for alternatives; Rudall 等人2009b)。在 Araceae，胚乳的初始分裂是高度不对称的，随后的细胞分裂最初只发生在珠孔室，该科被认为具有细胞胚乳(Tobe & Kadokawa，2010; 参见 Maheshwari & Khanna，1957)。这里的合点细胞有时是巨大的(例如 Paremeswaran 1959)。胚乳发育的初始不对称性是天南星科的特征，因此天南星科也可以被认为具有一种类似的胚乳; 菖蒲科也表现出类似的不对称性(Buell 1938)。微珠(如睡莲目)或微珠和合点端(多数来自合点端)结构域是否引起胚乳的体积也有差异。核胚乳发育的进化史也不清楚(Olsen 2004; 见 Zou 等人2001，了解其发育的微妙之处) ，而且在核胚乳发育方面也存在差异，例如在 Poaceae (Leroux 等人2014)。有关海球胚乳的进一步讨论，请参阅 Kaplan (1981)。

The beginning of a solution to such problems is to decompose these "types" into their underlying independent variables. Thus Blackmore et al. (2009) were able to decompose the pollen "types" used in Asteraceae into no fewer than 52 separate characters, while Dunning et al. (2017) found that an example of a reversal from C4 to C3 photosynthesis did not hold up when the independant variables that make up photosynthetic "types" were analysed (see also Floyd et al. 1999; Floyd & Friedman 2000; Herendeen & Miller 2000; Acosta et al. 2009; Y. Yang et al. 2014; Washburn et al. 2015; et al. 2015, etc.). Character states should be delimited only after analysis of the variation of that character at the level of the study being carried out. Thus delimiting states for a local study in the context of the variation shown by a character across all angiosperms may well be inappropriate since gaps in the variation shown by a particular feature in one clade may be obscured by variation in a completely unrelated clade - the universe problem.

这类问题的解决方案的开始是将这些“类型”分解为它们的底层自变量。因此 Blackmore 等人(2009年)能够将菊科中使用的花粉“类型”分解成不少于52个单独的字符，而 Dunning 等人(2017年)发现，当构成光合作用“类型”的独立变量被分析时，构成光合作用“类型”的一个从 C4到 C3光合作用逆转的例子并不成立(见 Floyd 等人1999年; Floyd & Friedman 2000年; herenden & Miller 2000年; Miller 等人2009年; Yang y. 等人2014年; Washburn 等人2015年; 等人2015年等)。性格状态只有在研究水平上分析了性格的变化之后才能进行界定。因此，在所有被子植物的特征变异的背景下为局部研究划定状态很可能是不恰当的，因为一个分支中特定特征所显示的变异的缺口可能被一个完全无关的分支的变异所掩盖——宇宙问题。

After we have decided on characters and states, there is then the not-so-small question of where character state changes should be placed on the tree, of ancestral state reconstruction/character optimisation. I am fitting characters to conservative trees that may have several polytomies. This makes optimisation of characters, that is, the assigment of character state change to a particular place on the tree, difficult (e.g. Madison & Madison 2002). In nearly all studies of the evolution of characters (D. Soltis et al. 2005b is a good example), the distributions of those characters are optimised on more or less fully resolved trees, and the construction of supertrees may yield more detailed hypotheses of relationships (for supertrees, see e.g. Cotton and Wilkinson 2007, 2008; Buerki et al. 2010d and literature; also see the supermatrix approach). Of course, some nodes even on fully resolved trees and/or supertrees may have little support, and character optimisations will then carry correspondingly little conviction. Topological uncertainties are important here: If Tofieldiaceae are sister to the rest of Alismatales (e.g. Ross et al. 2015), then where the change from "cellular" to "helobial" endosperm should be placed on the tree is unclear. Either one gain (apomorphy for order) and one loss (Araceae), or two gains (Tofieldiaceae, and above Araceae). But the problem is broader, since helobial-type development also occurs in the ANITA grade (e.g. Rudall et al. 2009b). Similarly, is triploid endosperm a synapomorphy for all angiosperms or only for the [magnoliid + Chloranthaceae] [other angiosperms] clade (Friedman 2001a, b, 2006; Baroux et al. 2002)? Friedman et al. (2003a, esp. b) and Friedman and Williams (2003, 2004) incline towards the latter hypothesis - see especially Williams and Friedman (2004) and Friedman and Ryerson (2009). If Nymphaeales are sister to Amborellales (but see above), then diploid endosperm may be the ancestral condition, with triploid endosperm evolving in parallel in *Amborella* and above the ANITA grade - and a supporting argument here might be that *Amborella* has an embryo sac unique in the angiosperms. Simple parsimony, whether ACCTRAN or DELTRAN, helps little here since there are no outgroups (e.g. Friedman & Floyd 2001; Ronse De Craene et al. 2003). But aside from such uncertainty, even with genomic data trees may remain unresolved in places. In such situations thinking about character evolution is very difficult indeed, putting it mildly (see e.g. Koenen 2019 for the issues involved).

在我们决定了字符和状态之后，还有一个不小的问题，那就是字符状态改变应该放在树的哪个位置，祖先状态重建/字符优化。我的角色适合保守的树木，可能有几个多切口。这使得字符的优化，也就是说，字符状态的分配改变为树上的特定位置，变得困难(例如 Madison & Madison 2002)。在几乎所有关于人物进化的研究中(d. Soltis 等人，2005b 是一个很好的例子) ，这些人物的分布在或多或少完全分解的树上最优化，超树的构建可能产生更详细的关系假设(对于超树，见 Cotton 和 Wilkinson，2007,2008; Buerki 等人，2010d 和文献; 也见超矩阵方法)。当然，有些节点甚至在完全分解的树和/或超树上也可能没有什么支持，因此字符优化也相应地没有什么说服力。拓扑不确定性在这里很重要: 如果土芥科植物是泽泻目其余植物的姐妹(例如 Ross 等人，2015年) ，那么应该在树上放置从“细胞”到“海球”胚乳的变化是不清楚的。无论是一个收益(为目的吗啡)和一个损失(天南星科) ，或两个收益(玉簪科，以上天南星科)。但是这个问题更广泛，因为在 ANITA 等级中也出现了阳生物型发育(例如 Rudall et al. 2009b)。类似地，三倍体胚乳是所有被子植物的突触形态还是仅仅是[玉兰科 + 金粟兰科][其他被子植物]支系的突触形态(Friedman 2001a，b，2006; Baroux et al. 2002) ？弗里德曼等(2003a，esp。弗里德曼和威廉姆斯(2003年和2004年)倾向于后一种假说——特别是威廉姆斯和弗里德曼(2004年)和弗里德曼和瑞尔森(2009年)。如果 Nymphaeales 是 amborelales 的姐妹(见上文) ，那么二倍体胚乳可能是原始状态，三倍体胚乳在 Amborella 平行进化，高于 ANITA 等级——这里的一个支持论点可能是 Amborella 有一个被子植物中独一无二的胚囊。简单的节约，不管是 ACCTRAN 还是 DELTRAN，在这里帮助不大，因为没有外部团体(例如 Friedman & Floyd 2001; Ronse De Craene et al. 2003)。但是除了这种不确定性，即使有了基因组数据树在某些地方可能仍然没有得到解决。在这种情况下，考虑角色的进化确实是非常困难的，说得委婉一点(例如，参见 koen2019的相关问题)。

Indeed, using either Bayesian or maximum likelihood analyses, making apparently reasonable suggestions about weighting gains over losses (or vice versa), or more complex assumptions along similar lines, or just using the rather simple models of evolution explicit in ACCTRAN or DELTRAN to place the character on the tree (e.g. Donoghue & Ackerley 1996; Cunningham et al. 1998; Omland 1997, 1999; Ree & Donoghue 1999; Polly 2001; Webster & Purvis 2001; Ronquist 2004; Crisp & Cook 2005; Remizowa et al. 2010b; Sokoloff et al. 2013d; O'Meara 2012; Gascuel & Steel 2014; Wortley et al. 2015; Sauquet et al. 2017; Parkins-Fukuchi 2017) may greatly affect the position of synapomorphies on trees, and hence our ideas of evolution. Sannier et al. (2007) give a good example concerning where on a tree one might peg changes in microsporogenesis in palms (see also Sannier et al. 2009), while Syme and Oakley (2012) note that some methods allow reversals much more easily than others. Pedersen et al. (2007) discuss the sometimes very substantial effect of node support on the posterior probabilities of ancestral character states. But, as Wortley et al. (2015: p. 195) noted rather sadly about optimization, "In general, characters that were unambiguously optimized in all contingencies were either those for which little data were available... or those known to be variable only within a single group, ...". If not reporting on other studies, here I think in terms of parsimony optimization, not always as explicit as it might be, but I have tried to indicate uncertainties as to where particularly important characters change on the tree.

事实上，使用贝叶斯分析或最大似然分析，提出明显合理的建议，衡量收益的损失(或反之亦然) ，或更复杂的假设沿类似的路线，或只是使用相当简单的演化模型明确在 ACCTRAN 或 DELTRAN 放置的特征树(e).G.1996; Cunningham et al. 1998; Omland 1997,1999; Ree & Donoghue 1999; Polly 2001; Webster & Purvis 2001;2004; Crisp & Cook 2005; Remizowa et al. 2010b; Sokoloff et al. 2013d; o’meara 2012; Gascuel & Steel 2014; Wortley et al. 2015; Sauquet et al. 2017; Parkins-Fukuchi 2017)可能会极大地影响树上的突触遗传的位置，因此我们的进化观念。Sannier 等人(2007年)举了一个很好的例子，说明在树上哪里可能会出现小孢子发生的变化(参见 Sannier 等人2009年) ，而 Syme 和 Oakley (2012年)指出，有些方法比其他方法更容易出现逆转。Pedersen 等人(2007)讨论了有时候节点支持对祖先特征状态的后验概率非常重要的影响。但是，正如 Wortley 等人(2015: p. 195)关于优化相当悲哀地指出的那样，“一般来说，在所有偶然事件中被明确优化的字符要么是那些只有很少数据可用的字符... ... 要么是那些已知只在一个组中变量的字符... ...”。如果不报道其他的研究，这里我认为在节俭优化方面，并不总是像它可能是明确的，但我试图指出不确定性，特别重要的字符在树上的变化。

Thus simple parsimony is just one of the ways to optimise the positions of character state changes on a tree, and it may not be the best. Different analyses of the same data may result in state changes ending up in different places on the tree, and/or there may be very different numbers of state changes, and/or changes are interpreted as probabilities given what what we know about the evolution of the character, branch lengths of the tree, topological uncertainties of that tree, and the like. Recent examples are studies of pollen morphology (Wright & Hillis 2014; Wortley et al. 2015; Lu et al. 2015) and of the construction of the ancestral angiosperm flower (Sauquet et al. 2017), where parsimony, maximum likelihood and Bayesian analyses are all compared. Sauquet et al. (2017: Supplementary Methods) capture the issues well, e.g. "MP... has the attractive property that no assumption is made on the relationship between change and branch length; ... Conversely, ML and rjMCMC results are conditional on the assumption that rates of morphological change are constant through times and across lineages." Despite this apparent attractive property of MP, the behaviour of ML and rjMCMC methods was seen as an "advantage" (ibid.). However, molecular clocks are somewhat out of favour these days, and the reasons for invoking a morphological clock, as in ML and rjMCMC methods, are unclear. The bottom line here is that every method has its problems, and extreme care is needed when using them.

因此，简单的节俭只是优化树中字符状态变化位置的方法之一，而且可能不是最好的方法。对同一数据的不同分析可能会导致状态变化最终出现在树的不同位置，并且/或者可能会有非常不同的状态变化数量，而且/或者变化被解释为概率，因为我们知道特征的进化、树的分支长度、树的拓扑不确定性等等。最近的例子是花粉形态的研究(Wright & Hillis 2014; Wortley 等人2015; Lu 等人2015)和被子植物祖先花的构造(Sauquet 等人2017) ，其中吝啬，最大可能性和贝叶斯分析都是比较。Sauquet 等人(2017: Supplementary Methods)很好地抓住了这个问题，例如“ MP... 具有吸引力的性质，即没有假设变化和分支长度之间的关系; ... 反过来，ML 和 rjMCMC 的结果是有条件的，假设形态变化的速率是不变的，通过时间和跨谱系。”尽管 MP 具有这种明显的吸引特性，ML 和 rjMCMC 方法的行为仍被视为一种“优势”(同上).然而，分子时钟在这些天有些不受欢迎，并且调用形态时钟的原因，如在 ML 和 rjMCMC 方法，是不清楚的。这里的底线是每个方法都有它的问题，并且在使用它们的时候需要非常小心。

A final point is that data must remain easily accessible and should cumulate, that is, information for variation in all characters across all flowering plants (say) should be freely available, be added to as new publications appear, and be linked to place of publication and specimens examined. In the context of such database both classifications and the meanings of botanical terms should be standardized. At first sight this might seem an unattainable, almost laughable goal. However, ecologists seem to be showing the way with [TRY Plant Trait database](https://www.try-db.org/TryWeb/Home.php) (see Kattge et al. 2011; Kissling et al. 2018), traits like wood density, growth form and photosynthetic pathway, which on 20.x.2019 included 11,850,781 trait records from 279,875 species of plants, and more local databases such as [PalmTraits 1.0](https://doi.org/10.5061/dryad.ts45225) (Kissling et al. 2019) are being developed - and the data will also be part of TRY. Along these lines, it has long struck me how little the more taxonomic side of out business has to show for over 250 years of work - most information in the majority of species descriptions cannot be linked to particular specimens. However, recent attempts to work out the floral morphology of the ancestral angiosperm () and to understand various aspects of early angioperm evolution (e.g.) are associated with

最后一点是，数据必须保持容易访问和应累积，也就是说，所有被子植物的所有字符的变化信息(比如说)应免费提供，随着新出版物的出现而添加，并与出版地点和样本检查相关联。在这种数据库的背景下，植物学术语的分类和含义都应该标准化。乍一看，这似乎是一个遥不可及、几乎可笑的目标。然而，生态学家似乎用 TRY 植物性状数据库(见 Kattge 等人2011年; Kissling 等人2018年)展示了这种方式，木材密度、生长形态和光合途径等性状，在2019年20月20日的报告中包括了来自279,875种植物的11,850,781个性状记录，以及更多的本地数据库，如 PalmTraits 1.0(Kissling 等人2019年)正在开发中，这些数据也将成为 TRY 的一部分。沿着这些思路，我长期以来一直感到震惊的是，在250多年的研究工作中，我们的业务中更多的分类学方面几乎没有显示出什么——大多数物种描述中的大多数信息都不能与特定的标本联系起来。然而，最近试图解决的祖先被子植物的花形态()和了解早期被子植物进化的各个方面(例如)是相关的

The take-home message?: We make the botanical terms we use, not "nature". For me, seeing a plant is forgetting the names its parts are called (with apologies to Weschler 2009); different botanical terms used for what seems to be the same structure are flags that there may be variation out there, but not necessarily much more. As Hesse et al. (2009b: p. 27) observed, "Nature itself neither needs categories nor has any knowledge of categories". More particularly, as Olsen (2004: p. S215) noted, "In spite of recent progress in understanding angiosperm phylogeny, all of the main questions regarding the evolutionary history of the nuclear endosperm remain unresolved." - and this is still the case.

带回家的信息？例如我们使用的植物学术语，不是“自然”。对我来说，看到一株植物就是忘记了它的部分的名字(向 Weschler 2009致歉) ; 不同的植物学术语用来描述似乎是同一结构的东西，这些标志可能有变化，但不一定有更多。正如 Hesse 等人(2009年 b: 第27页)指出的那样，“自然本身既不需要分类，也不需要任何分类知识”。更具体地说，正如 Olsen (2004: p. S215)所指出的，“尽管最近在被子植物系统发育的理解上取得了进展，所有关于核胚乳进化历史的主要问题仍然没有得到解决。”现在情况依然如此。

There are six final points to remember about the characterisations below, and descriptions in general:

关于下面的人物特征，还有六点需要记住，以及一般的描述:

1\. I have been much more generally comparative in the ultimate characterisations than is perhaps strictly necessary. That is, the user will be able to find information on the variation of most characters mentioned in the character list as it occurs in all families. An example is leaf ptyxis, which seems to characterise only a few or the terminal groups recognised here, although I have tried to include information about it more generally.

1.在最终的性格特征方面，我的比较性要比严格意义上的必要性大得多。也就是说，用户将能够找到关于字符列表中提到的大多数字符的变化的信息，因为它发生在所有的家庭。一个例子就是树叶习性，它似乎只描述了这里所认识的几个或者几个终结群，尽管我已经尝试包含更广泛的关于它的信息。

2\. More conventional descriptions of a family, for example, as in Cronquist (1981), include a mixture of plesiomorphies and apomorphies at various levels, including apomorphies of groups of genera, or even individual genera, within the family. Although it is difficult to disentangle the importance of the features listed (but typographic conventions, as in Judd et al. 2002, 2015, help), they better convey a description of the organism as a whole. Nevertheless, by summarizing the relevant part of the character state hierarchy before each ordinal characterization, I perhaps give something of the same effect.

图2。例如，在 Cronquist (1981)中，对一个家族的更为传统的描述包括各个层次上的纹理图谱和非纹理图谱的混合，其中包括科内属群或甚至个别属的非纹理图谱。虽然很难区分所列特征的重要性(但是排版约定，如 Judd 等人2002,2015，help) ，他们更好地传达了对整个有机体的描述。尽管如此，通过总结每个序号角色塑造之前的人物状态层次结构的相关部分，我也许会给出一些相同的效果。

3\. Some of the features in the characterisations simply describe the extent of variation within the clade, e.g., "stomata anomocytic or paracytic". This is particularly common when relationships within a family, or between a family and its immediate relatives, are unclear. Features so described will not often turn out to be synapomorphies, although elements of the variation they encompass may.

图3。特征中的一些特征只是简单地描述了分支内的变异程度，例如“气孔异常细胞或平列”。当一个家庭内部或者家庭与其直系亲属之间的关系不清楚时，这种情况尤其常见。这样描述的特征通常不会被证明是突触遗传学，尽管它们包含的变异元素可能。

4\. There may seem to be little "biology" in the lists of characters at the beginning of each page here. In this context, I am reminded of Stebbins's review of Cronquist (1981) which read in its entirety "The only material of even peripheral interest to the general evolutionist consists of short commentaries on family relationships placed at the end of the description [sic] of many of the families" (Stebbins 1982: p. 628). However, there may be more of interest if you go to the appropriate place in the hierarchy, even if we know little about the functional or adaptive significance of many synapomorphies. Apart from some wind-pollinated, aquatic and parasitic taxa, it is usually difficult to characterise larger groups ecologically, although clades like most of Ericaceae are exceptions. Indeed, much of the "biology" in more conventional descriptions comes from mention of the pollination biology, for example, of particular genera and other small groups within a family, and users can add this emphasis here as they focus on the taxa that grow locally. However, information on more general aspects of ecophysiology, divergence and/or diversification, pollination and fruit dispersal, and associations with particular groups of herbivores, bacteria and fungi, etc., is being added as it becomes available.

图4。在每一页开头的字符列表中，似乎没有什么“生物学”的东西。在这方面，我想起了斯特宾斯对克朗奎斯特(1981)的评论，其全文是:”对一般进化论者甚至是次要的兴趣的唯一材料包括放在许多家庭描述[原文如此]末尾的关于家庭关系的简短评论”(斯特宾斯1982年: 第628页)。然而，如果您进入层次结构中的适当位置，可能会有更多的兴趣，即使我们对许多突触遗传学的功能性或适应性重要性知之甚少。除了一些风媒传粉，水生和寄生分类群，它通常很难具有更大的群体生态学特征，虽然像大多数杜鹃花科的分支是例外。事实上，传统描述中的“生物学”大多来自于授粉生物学的提及，例如，某个科中的特定属和其他小群体，使用者可以在这里增加这种强调，因为他们专注于生长在当地的分类群。然而，关于生理生态学、分化和/或多样化、授粉和果实扩散以及与特定的食草动物、细菌和真菌等群体的关系等更一般方面的资料正在增加。

5\. As we find out more about variation we find fewer and fewer features that are constant throughout a group. Most unqualified statements of presence and absence should properly be qualified as "usually present" or "usually absent" if one is thinking of the characterisations as encompassing the total variation within a clade. Thus *Pistia*, alone among monocots as so far known, has sieve tube plastids with starch grains, not protein crystals, although the latter is indeed an apomorphy for monocots. Just about all characters that are high-level apomorphies reverse and/or occur in parallel several times on the tree. Thus Reyes et al. (2018) found that monosymmetry originated at least 148 times in angiosperms, and has reversed 69 times or so, and there was widespread parallelism in the other four characters that they examined. Some taxa in Malvaceae-Sterculioideae and Ranunculaceae are effectively gymnospermous...

5.当我们发现更多关于变化的信息时，我们发现越来越少的特征在整个群体中保持不变。大多数无保留的存在和不存在的陈述应该恰当地限定为”通常存在”或”通常不存在”，如果人们认为特征包括一个支系内的总变化。因此，目前已知的单子叶植物中，只有鱼类具有由淀粉颗粒构成的筛管质体，而不是蛋白质晶体，尽管蛋白质晶体确实是单子叶植物的一种类质同晶体。几乎所有高级自同步字符都会反向和/或并行地在树上多次出现。因此，Reyes 等人(2018年)发现，单对称性在被子植物中起源至少148次，反转了69次左右，他们研究的其他四个特征有广泛的平行性。广义的苹果科-梧桐亚科和毛茛科中的一些分类群是有效的裸子植物。

6\. Fossils may have character combinations unknown in extant taxa, as may be seen in the discussions of Fagaceae, Platanaceae, Iteaceae and Calycanthaceae, for example. How this will affect characters at interior nodes remains to be seen. Moreover, where exactly on the tree a particular fossil is to be placed can be difficult to work out - see Nymphaeaceae, Calycanthaceae, Paracryphiaceae, etc., fossils such as *Archaefructus* and *Silvianthemum* posing particular problems.

图6。在现存的分类群中，化石可能具有未知的特征组合，例如在有关 Fagaceae、白菜科、意大利科和花萼科的讨论中可以看到这一点。这将如何影响字符在内部节点仍然有待观察。此外，确切地放置在树上一个特定的化石可能很难确定-看睡莲科，花萼科，假泪科等化石，如古石榴和银线菊提出了特定的问题。

The bottom line is that our morphological, anatomical and chemical knowledge of many critical taxa is woefully incomplete, and much basic - and unfortunately perhaps unfashionable - work must be carried to clarify the distribution of morphological, anatomical and chemical characters. For excellent examples of what can to be done, see the work of P. K. Endress, W. E. Friedman, P. Leins and C. Erbar, L.-P. Ronse de Craene and H. Tobe and all their collaborators (various aspects of floral morphology and development) and S. R. Jensen and collaborators (iridoids). Really remarkable discoveries continue to be made, for instance, the realization that the "typical" 8-ncleate embryo sac is not found in basal angiosperms (e.g. Friedman 2001a), and the description of the embryology of *Cardiopteris*, related to holly, that shows it to be without parallel in any other flowering plant (Tobe 2016). Indeed, filling in the gaps in our knowledge of more mundane things like nodal anatomy, cell and tissue distributions, stomatal morphology, seed coat anatomy, and the like can be quite easy (see also [below](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/introductionnew.htm#missingdata)) and will clarify our understanding of evolution. Much effort must continue to be spent in summarizing characters of well-established clades at all levels, providing features by which they may be recognized, and signaling synapomorphies. However, given our current understanding of both phylogenies and morphology, how to relate the two is not that simple, and different assumptions about character evolution may greatly affect the position of synapomorphies on trees. Nevertheless, it is a relatively easy matter to update notes such as these and to incorporate data on characters that have never before been considered in the context of a tree.

归根结底，我们对许多关键分类群的形态、解剖和化学知识是不幸地不完整的，许多基本的工作——不幸的是可能不流行——必须进行，以澄清形态、解剖和化学特征的分布。有关可以做什么的优秀例子，请参阅 p. k. Endress、 w. e. Friedman、 p. Leins 和 c. Erbar、 L.-P 的著作。Ronse de Craene 和 h. Tobe 及其合作者(花形态学和发育的各个方面)和 s. r. Jensen 及其合作者(环烯醚萜)。真正引人注目的发现还在继续，例如，人们意识到“典型的”8ncleate 胚胎囊不存在于基生被子植物中(例如 Friedman 2001a) ，以及对 Cardiopteris 胚胎学的描述(与冬青有关) ，表明它在任何其他开花植物中都是独一无二的(Tobe 2016)。事实上，填补我们知识中的空白，比如节点解剖学、细胞和组织分布、气孔形态学、种皮解剖学等等，可以非常容易(另见下文) ，并澄清我们对进化的理解。必须继续投入大量精力，总结各级已经确立的分支的特征，提供可以识别这些特征的特征，并将这些特征传递给突触遗传学。然而，鉴于我们目前对系统发育和形态学的理解，如何将两者联系起来并不是那么简单，而且关于性状进化的不同假设可能会极大地影响突触遗传在树上的位置。尽管如此，更新这样的注释并加入以前从未在树的上下文中考虑过的字符数据还是相对容易的。

**SUMMARY OF THE SYSTEM**
[Back to Top](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/introductionnew.htm#top)

系统摘要[返回页首]

Below is a summary of the relationships within orders of all the families of seed plants; there are direct links to the pages where the families are discussed. Families, etc., accepted in A.P.G. IV (2016) and the most recent edition of *The Plant Book* (Mabberley 2017) are very largely the same as those below.

下面是所有种子植物家族内部关系的摘要; 有直接链接到讨论这些家族的页面。在 a.p.g. IV (2016)和最新版《植物图书》(Mabberley 2017)中接受的家庭等基本上与下面的一样。

However, there are a few changes in relationships and new families/orders that have been made since APG IV. The latter are listed immediately below, while in the summary they are indicated by asterisks. Some of these changes are new families that reflect recent collections, e.g. the remarkable Tiganophytaceae, from the Namib area and in Brassicales, while others, like Oncothecales, a very small order that is sister to all other core asterids/gentianids, are the results of changed ideas of relationships that are being suggested by comprehensive analyses using nuclear genomes. This latter kind of change in particular is being made only when support for the changed relationships is strong, otherwise confusion will result. Note that many relationships along the spine of the Pentapetalae well up into the asterids are subject to change! All changes are being carefully justified.

然而，自第四届亚太经社会会议以来，在人际关系和新的家庭/秩序方面发生了一些变化。后者立即列在下面，而在摘要中，它们由星号表示。其中一些变化是反映最近收集的新科，例如来自纳米布地区和 Brassicales 的著名的提加植物科，而另一些变化，例如 Oncothecales，一个非常小的目，是所有其他星群/龙胆科核心的姊妹目，是由于利用核基因组进行综合分析而提出的关系观念的变化。特别是后一种变化只有在对变化的关系的支持很强时才会发生，否则就会产生混乱。请注意，沿着 Pentapetalae 脊柱向上延伸到星号的许多关系都可能会发生变化！所有的改变都被仔细地证明是正确的。

Square brackets - [...] - enclose clades; the plus sign - + - designates terminal sister taxa; a comma - , - denotes part of a polytomy.

方括号-[ ... ]-括起来的分支; 加号-+-表示末端的姊妹分类单元; 逗号-,-表示息肉切除术的一部分。

[Lamiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/lamialesweb.htm#Lamiaceae) [Mazaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/lamialesweb.htm#Mazus) [Phrymaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/lamialesweb.htm#Phrymaceae) [Paulowniaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/lamialesweb.htm#Paulowniaceae) + [Wightiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/lamialesweb.htm#Wightiaceae)\*] + [Orobanchaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/lamialesweb.htm#Orobanchaceae)

[环生籽科][四粉草科科 + 木犀科][盘菌科[苦苣苔科 + 苦苣苔科][车前草科[玄参科][山茱萸科 + 木犀科][花梨科 + 马鞭草科] ,[狸藻科科[佛手瓜科[桐科 + 维吾尔科[] + 列当科]

**CAMPANULID/ASTERID II**
**[Cardiopteridales\* 心翼目 \*](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/cardiopteridalesweb.htm#Cardiopteridales)**

[Cardiopteridaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/cardiopteridalesweb.htm#Cardiopteridaceae) + [Stemonuraceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/cardiopteridalesweb.htm#Stemonuraceae)

[心翼果科 + 百部花科]

**[Escalloniales 七叶树属](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/Escalloniales.html#Escalloniales)**
