七角蕨科

**[Asterales 海星目](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Asterales)**

[Rousseaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Rousseaceae) + [Campanulaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Campanulaceae) [Pentaphragmataceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Pentaphragmataceae) [Stylidiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Stylidiaceae) [Alseuosmiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Alseuosmiaceae) [Phellinaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Phellinaceae) + [Argophyllaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Argophyllaceae) [ [Menyanthaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Menyanthaceae) [Goodeniaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Goodeniaceae) [Calyceraceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Calyceraceae) + [Asteraceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Asteraceae)

[罗赛科 + 桔梗科][五膜草科科][山楂科][山楂科][芦苇科 + 阿拉木科][芦苇科]

**[Bruniales 布鲁尼亚莱斯](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/brunialesweb.htm#Bruniales)**

苔藓科

**[Desfontainiales\* Desfontainiales \*](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/desfontainialesweb.htm#Desfontainiales)**

[Columelliaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/Desfontainialesweb.htm#Columelliaceae)

哥伦布科

**[Apiales 伞形目](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/apialesweb.htm#Apiales)**

[Pennantiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/apialesweb.htm#Pennantiaceae) [ [Torricelliaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/apialesweb.htm#Torricelliaceae) [Griseliniaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/apialesweb.htm#Griseliniaceae) [Pittosporaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/apialesweb.htm#Pittosporaceae) [Araliaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/apialesweb.htm#Araliaceae) [Myodocarpaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/apialesweb.htm#Myodocarpaceae) + [Apiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/apialesweb.htm#Apiaceae)

[狼尾草科[灰树科[海桐科[海桐科]

**[Paracryphiales 丙烯酰亚目](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/Paracryphiales.html#Paracryphiaceae)**

伞形科

**[Dipsacales 续断属](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/dipsacalesweb.htm#Dipsacales)**

[Viburnaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/dipsacalesweb.htm#Viburnaceae) + [Caprifoliaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/dipsacalesweb.htm#Caprifoliaceae)

[荚莲科 + 忍冬科]

**ON SOME POORLY-KNOWN TAXA THAT ARE IN URGENT NEED OF STUDY**
[Back to Top](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/introductionnew.htm#top)

关于一些急需研究的贫困类群[返回页首]

Although a vast amount of morphological s.l. information is being developed from question-driven research on model organisms like *Zea*, *Arabidopsis* and *Antirrhinum*, it is often difficult to know how far the results can be extrapolated. Indeed, I have long been impressed (or depressed) about several aspects about the general knowledge of morphology.

虽然大量的形态学 s.l. 信息正在开发从问题驱动的研究模式生物，如 Zea，拟南芥和 Antirrhinum，往往很难知道结果可以推断到多远。事实上，关于形态学的一般知识的几个方面，我长期以来一直对它印象深刻(或感到沮丧)。

— How little we really know when we discuss evolution - for most features, we extrapolate from a quite small data base.

ー当我们讨论进化论时，我们真正知道的是多么的少——对于大多数特征，我们是从一个相当小的数据库中推断出来的。

— How little morphological s.l. knowledge is added in most phylogenetic studies.

ー在大多数系统发育研究中，只增加了多少形态学方面的知识。

— How much we are dependent on general surveys from the 1880s to the 1930s in particular (for cytology and plant chemistry the surveys are later, but even here our knowledge base is increasing very slowly), although for aspects of floral morphology and development, for example, a few authors have added substantial amounts of data over the last thirty years. Fortunately, much of this older literature is now on line, for example, see the [Botanicus Digital Library](javascript:showImage('http://www.botanicus.org',600,500)), with approaching 2,500,000 pages scanned, while in the [Biodiversity Heritage Library](javascript:showImage('http://www.biodiversitylibrary.org',600,500)) there are about 46,000,000 pages [as of 13.iv.2015].

ー我们在多大程度上依赖于19世纪80年代至19世纪30年代的一般调查(尤其是细胞学和植物化学调查的时间较晚，但即使在这方面，我们的知识基础也增长非常缓慢) ，尽管在花的形态和发育方面，例如，一些作者在过去30年中增加了大量的数据。幸运的是，这些古老的文献现在大部分都在线了，例如，参见 Botanicus 数字图书馆，扫描了接近250万页，而在生物多样性文献图书馆图书馆里有大约46,000,000页。Iv. 2015].

— How easy it is to add new information about many organ systems.

ー添加关于许多器官系统的新信息是多么容易。

A more comprehensive understanding of plant morphology is needed to enable broad evolutionary questions to be answered with a greater degree of confidence. There is a particular need for targeted surveys of the morphological variation of particular groups. Given limited time and resources, one can also profitably focus on small clades an understanding of the morphology of which will have the greatest effect on our understanding of character evolution. These include taxa along the spines of branches, a small clade sister to the rest of a very speciose clade, etc.. Add to that a judicious sampling of more speciose clades (see also Endress 2011) carefully targeted in the context of the phylogeny of the group of interest; untargeted surveys, or surveys of groups whose phylogeny is unclear, may yield less of interest than one might hope (c. f. Schönenberger & von Balthazar 2006). **Neither phylogeny without good comparative morphological knowledge nor comparative morphology without a good phylogeny is of much use.**

我们需要对植物形态学更全面的理解，这样才能更有把握地回答更广泛的进化问题。特别需要对特定群体的形态变异进行有针对性的调查。在时间和资源有限的情况下，我们也可以把注意力放在对形态学的理解上，这对我们理解角色的进化有着最大的影响。这些分支包括沿着枝条刺的分类群，一个很小的姐妹分支到一个非常特殊的分支的其余分支，等等。此外，对更多的物种支系进行明智的抽样(参见 Endress 2011) ，仔细地根据相关群体的系统发育进行选择; 非目标性的调查，或者对系统发育不清的群体进行调查，可能不会产生人们所希望的那么大的兴趣(参见 sch ö nenberger & von Balthazar 2006)。没有良好的比较形态学知识的系统发育学和没有良好的系统发育学的比较形态学都没有多大用处。

To help in building up a more extensive information base that will facilitate our thinking about the larger patterns of flowering plant evolution, the list below includes a number of quite small taxa whose phylogenetic position is such that information on embryo sac development, chemistry, seed anatomy, etc., is particularly important for our understanding of the evolution of those features. The taxa listed are reasonable targets for comprehensive studies and are eminently suitable for Masters theses. Of course, given the current academic climate, I cannot say that such studies will be highly regarded by tenure and promotion committees (bless their hearts, wherever they might be), but they should nevertheless be integral to all phylogenetic studies that are concerned with character evolution and integral parts of grant proposals.

为了帮助建立一个更广泛的信息库，以便于我们思考开花植物进化的更大模式，下面的列表包括了一些相当小的分类群，它们的系统发育位置是这样的，胚囊发育、化学、种子解剖等信息对于我们理解这些特征的进化特别重要。所列出的分类单元是综合研究的合理对象，尤其适合硕士论文。当然，鉴于目前的学术环境，我不能说这些研究会受到终身任期和晋升委员会的高度重视(无论它们在哪里，请保佑它们) ，但它们应该是所有涉及性格演变和拨款申请不可分割的组成部分的系统发育研究的一部分。

The taxa listed below come from all over the world except the northern Temperate and Arctic zones. Tropical Africa (even excluding the Cape region and Madagascar), Central and tropical South America, and Australia-New Zealand are particularly well represented, East Asia and Indo-Malesia somewhat less so, then the Cape region, Madagascar, and the southern U.S.A./northern Mexico, and finally New Caledonia, temperate South America, and Europe. Although some of these genera like *Triceratella* (Commelinaceae) are very rare, others are quite common, or are even in cultivation (*Rehmannia*, *Aextoxicon*, *Portulaca*, etc.). Such a list does not pretend to be exhaustive, indeed, there are some genera that are quite well known, but for which important information is lacking - thus I know of no reports of fertilization from *Nothofagus* (Nothofagaceae, sister to rest of Fagales). Given our general level of knowledge, there is no shortage of plants to look at!

下面列出的分类群来自世界各地，除了北温带和北极地区。热带非洲(甚至不包括开普地区和马达加斯加) ，中南美洲和热带南美洲，以及 Australia-New Zealand 特别多，东亚和 Indo-Malesia 少一些，然后是开普地区，马达加斯加，美国南部/墨西哥北部，最后是新喀里多尼亚，温带的南美洲和欧洲。虽然这些属中有些是非常罕见的(鸭跖草科) ，其他是相当普遍的，甚至在栽培(地黄，Aextoxicon，Portulaca 等)。这样的名单并不是详尽无遗的，的确，有一些属是相当知名的，但是缺乏重要的信息——因此我没有听说过野山毛榉(Nothofagaceae，Fagales 的姐妹)受精的报告。考虑到我们的一般知识水平，我们并不缺乏植物可供参考！

In addition to the taxa listed, many others, especially in Geraniales, practically the whole of Phytolaccaceae and Molluginaceae, Irvingiaceae, Kirkiaceae, Acanthaceae-Nelsonioideae, Escalloniaceae, Bruniaceae, etc., could well have been included, and as phylogenies in Lamiales, etc., become better resolved, other clades in urgent need of study will become apparent. Many holoparasites need developmental and embryological studies.

除了列出的分类单元外，还有许多其他的分类单元，特别是在 Geraniales，实际上整个的商陆科和墨尔本科，鸢尾科，Kirkiaceae，爵床科-莲心亚科，七叶树科，苔藓科，等等，都可能被包括在内，并且随着 Lamiales 等分类系统的进展，变得更加清晰，其他迫切需要研究的分支将变得更加明显。许多全寄生虫需要进行发育学和胚胎学研究。

Mention of “basal” in the comments below is relative; it means basal in a tree relative to other more speciose clades, or a small clade sister to a very speciose clade; there are no implications that members of such clades are “primitive” or plesiomorphic.

在下面的注释中提到“基底”是相对的; 它意味着相对于其他更多的分支而言，它在一棵树中是“基底”的，或者是一个非常特殊的分支的一个小的姐妹分支; 这种分支的成员是“原始的”或者是同形的没有暗示。

[Achatocarpaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Achatocarpaceae): Caryophyllales. *Achatocarpus* (Mexico to Argentina) *Phaulothamnus* (S.W. U.S.A., N. Mexico): 10 and 1 spp. respectively. Sister to Amaranthaceae s.l.

瘦果科: 石竹目。瘦果目(墨西哥到阿根廷) Phaulothamnus -LRB- S.W. U.S.A. ，墨西哥分别为10和1个。

[Aextoxicaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/berberidopsidalesweb.html#Aextoxicaceae): Berberidopsidales. *Aextoxicon* (Chile): 1 sp. One of two families in Berberidopsidales, along spine below the asterids, see also Berberidopsidaceae.

亚麻科: 智利藤目。亚麻科(智利) : 1 sp. 亚麻属的一个科，沿着智利藤目下面的脊柱，见智利藤科。

[Aizoaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Aizoaceae): Caryophyllales. *Acrosanthes* (Western Cape, South Africa): 6 spp. The only genus in its subfamily.

Aizoaceae: 石竹目。顶角目(南非西开普省) : 6个。是该亚科中唯一的属。

[Akaniaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/brassicalesweb.htm#Akaniaceae): Brassicales. *Akania* (E. Australia), *Bretschneidera* (S.E. Asia): 1 and 1 spp. respectively. With Tropaeolaceae, sister to all other Brassicales.

赤藓科: 十字花科。赤藓目(澳大利亚) ，伯乐树(东南亚) : 分别为1和1。与金莲科为姊妹目。

[Alseuosmiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Alseuosmiaceae): Asterales. *Alseuosmia* (New Zealand), *Crispiloba* (N.E. Australia), *Periomphale* (New Caledonia), *Platyspermation* (New Caledonia), *Wittsteinia* (S.E. Australia, New Guinea): 5, 1, 1, 1, and 2 spp. respectively.

八角蕨科: 菊目。新西兰、澳大利亚、新喀里多尼亚、新西兰、新西兰、澳大利亚、新几内亚分别为5、1、1、1和2个单位。

[Anacampserotaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Anacampserotaceae): Caryophyllales. *Anacampseros*, *Avonia*, *Grahamia* (Africa, S.W. U.S.A., Central and South America, Australia, very scattered): 32 spp. in whole family. Sister to Cactaceae.

八脉蕨科: 石竹目。阿纳坎普塞罗斯，Avonia，格拉哈米亚(非洲，S.W. U.S.A. ，中美洲和南美洲，澳大利亚，非常分散) : 全家32人。仙人掌科的姐妹。

[Aphanopetalaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/saxifragalesweb.htm#Aphanopetalaceae): Saxifragales. *Aphanopetalum* (W. and E. Australia): 2 spp.

胶藤科: 虎耳草属。无瓣悬铃木(西澳大利亚和东澳大利亚) : 2 spp。

[Aphloiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/crossosomatalesweb.htm#Aphloiaceae): Crossosomatales. *Aphloia* (E. Africa, Madagascar, Seychelles): 1-several spp. Sister to one major clade in the order.

口疮科: 交叉口疮目。口疮属(非洲东部，马达加斯加，塞舌尔) : 1-几个口疮。一个主要支序的姐妹。

[Asteraceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Asteraceae): Asterales. *Corymbium* (South Africa); 7 spp. Sister to Asteroideae.

菊科: 菊目。伞房花属(南非) ; 7株。菊亚科姐妹花。

[Asteropeiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Asteropeiaceae): Caryophyllales. *Asteropeia* (Madagascar): 8 spp. One family of two in clade sister to core Caryophyllales, see also Physenaceae.

菊科: 石竹目。菊科(马达加斯加) : 8个。石竹目的姐妹分支中的一个两个家族，也见植物门科。

[Barbeuiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Barbeuiaceae): Caryophyllales. *Barbeiua* (Madagascar): 1 sp. Sister to a very speciose part of Caryophyllales.

石竹科: 石竹目。石竹目(马达加斯加) : 1 sp. Caryophyllales 一个非常特殊部分的姐妹。

[Barbeyaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/rosalesweb.htm#Barbeyaceae): Rosales. *Barbeya* (Horn of Africa, Arabia): 1 sp. Near Rhamnaceae.

芭比亚科: 蔷薇科。芭比亚(非洲之角，阿拉伯) : 1种。近鼠李科。

[Berberidopsidaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/berberidopsidalesweb.html#Berberidopsidaceae): Berberidopsidales. *Streptothamnus* (E. Australia): 1 sp., florally very different from *Berberidopsis*. One of two families in Berberidopsidales, along spine below the asterids, see also Aextoxicaceae.

智利藤科: 智利藤目。链球菌(澳大利亚) : 1种，在植物区系上与 Berberidopsis 非常不同。智利藤目的两个科中的一个，沿着小星星下面的脊柱，也参见 aextoicaceae。

[Bixaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/malvalesweb.htm#Diegodendraceae): Malvales. *Diegodendron* (Madagascar): 1 sp. Isolated in Bixaceae.

比克斯科: 麦花科。马达加斯加卷叶蝉属(马达加斯加) : 1属。分布于 Bixaceae。

[Brassicaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/brassicalesweb.htm#Brassicaceae): Brassicales. *Aethionema* (Mediterranean to Afghanistan): 70 spp. Sister to all other Brassicaceae.

十字花科: 十字花科。地中海至阿富汗) : 70株。是所有其他十字花科植物的姐妹。

[Buxaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/buxalesweb.htm#Didymelaceae): Buxales. *Didmyeles* (Madagascar): 2 spp. Sister to rest of family.

黄杨科: 黄杨目。马达加斯加岛分布: 2个。其余家系的姐妹。

[Carlemanniaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/lamialesweb.htm#Carlemanniaceae): Lamiales - sister to Oleaceae, together sister to the rest of the order, minus one species! *Carlemannia*, *Silvianthus* (both S.E. Asia to W. Malesia): 3 and 1 spp. respectively.

山茱萸科: 山茱萸属-木犀科的姐妹，一起姐妹为其余目，负一种！卡列曼尼亚，西尔维安瑟斯(都是 S.E. Asia 到马里西亚) : 3和1 spp。

[Campanulaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Campanulaceae): Asterales. Cyphioideae: *Cyphia* (Africa): 60 spp. Cyphocarpoideae: *Cyphocarpus* (Chile): 2 spp. Nemacladoideae: *Nemocladus* (S.W. North America): 12 spp. Basal or nearly so in the family.

桔梗科: 菊目。囊藻亚科: 囊藻(非洲) : 60个。Cyphocarpoideae: Cyphocarpus (智利) : 2 spp。线虫亚科: 南美洲线虫亚科: 12种。在家族中基部的或近基本如此。

[Campynemataceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/lilialesweb.htm#Campynemataceae): Liliales. *Campynema* (Tasmania), *Campynemanthe* (New Caledonia, somewhat known): 1 and 3 spp. respectively.

弯曲线虫科: 百合目。弯曲线虫科(塔斯马尼亚) ，弯曲线虫科(喀里多尼亚，有点名气) : 分别为1和3。

[Caprifoliaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/dipsacalesweb.htm#Caprifoliaceae): Dipsacales. *Zabelia* (East Asia, Afghanistan to Japan): 6 spp. Crucial position in middle of Caprifoliaceae.

忍冬科: 川续断目。忍冬属(东亚，阿富汗到日本) : 6个孢子。忍冬科中部关键位置。

[Caryocaraceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/malpighialesweb.htm#Caryocaraceae): Malpighiales. *Anthodiscus* (tropical South America), *Caryocar* (Central America, tropical South America): 8 and 15 spp. respectively.

核果科: 麦芽目。花柄目(热带南美洲) ，核果目(中美洲，热带南美洲) : 分别8和15个单位。

[Centroplacaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/malpighialesweb.htm#Centroplacaceae): Malpighiales. *Centroplacus* (West Africa), *Bhesa* (Indomalesia): 1 and 5 spp. respectively.

积雪草科: 积雪草目。积雪草目(西非) ，百合科: 分别为1和5。

[Codonaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/boraginalesweb.htm#Codonaceae): Boraginales. *Codon* (South Africa): 2 spp. Sister to clade including Boraginaceae.

齿蕨科: 紫草目。密码子目(南非) : 2 spp. 。包括紫草科的姐妹。

[Combretaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/myrtalesweb2.htm#Combretaceae): Myrtales. *Strephonema* (West Africa): 3 spp. Sister to rest of family.

紫穗槐科: 紫薇属。紫穗槐属(西非) : 3株。是其余家系的姐妹。

[Commelinaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/commelinalesweb.htm#Commelinaceae): Commelinales. *Cartonema* (N. and S.W. Australia, New Guinea) and probably *Triceratella* (Zimbabwe): 11 and 1 spp. respectively. In clade sister to rest of family.

鸭跖目: 鸭跖目。Cartonema (n. 和 s.w. 澳大利亚，新几内亚)和 tricoratella (津巴布韦)分别为11和1个单位。在世系中姐妹为其余的家族。

[Convolvulaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/solanalesweb.htm#Convolvulaceae): Solanales. *Humbertia* (Madagascar): 1 sp. Sister to rest of family.

旋花科: 茄属。马达加斯加: 1属。其余家系的姐妹。

[Cordiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/boraginalesweb.htm#Cordiaceae): Boraginales. *Hoplestigma* (West Africa). 1 spp. Strange floral morphology.

茜草科: 紫草目。菊科(西非)。1个孢子。奇怪的花形态。

[Ctenolophonaceaee](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/malpighialesweb.htm#Ctenolophonaceae): Malpighiales. *Ctenolophon* (tropical West Africa, Malesia): 3 spp.

麻雀: 麻雀目。麻雀目(西非热带，麻雀岛) : 3个单位。

[Cucurbitaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/cucurbitalesweb.htm#Cucurbitaceae): Cucurbitales. *Indofevillea* (N. E. India, Assam, Tibet, Myanmar): 2 spp. Sister to all other Cucurbitoideae.

葫芦科: 葫芦目。印度东北部，阿萨姆邦，西藏，缅甸) : 2个，其他葫芦亚科的姐妹。

[Curtisiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/cornalesweb.htm#Curtisiaceae): Cornales. *Curtisia* (Southern Africa): 1 sp.

莪术科: 山茱萸目。莪术(南非) : 1属。

[Cyrillaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/ericalesweb.htm#Cyrillaceae): Ericales. *Cliftonia* (S.E. U.S.A), *Cyrilla* (S. U.S.A. to N. South America): 1 and 1 spp. respectively. Sister to Ericaceae.

杜鹃花科: 杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科，杜鹃花科,。

[Dasypogonaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/arecalesweb.htm#Dasypogonaceae): Arecales. *Baxteria* (S.W. Australia), *Calectasia* (S.E. Australia), *Dasypogon* (S.W. Australia), *Kingia* (S.W. Australia): 1, 11, 3, and 1 spp. respectively. ?Sister to Arecaceae.

毛蕊花科: 槟榔目。巴克斯特里亚(澳大利亚东南部) ，卡勒克塔西亚(澳大利亚东南部) ，达西波贡(澳大利亚东南部) ，金吉亚(澳大利亚东南部)分别为1,11,3和1。？槟榔科的姐妹。

[Dipentodontaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/huertealesweb.htm#Dipentodontaceae): Huerteales. *Dipentodon* (E. Asia), *Perrottetia* (Central and W. South America, S.E. Asia to Australia): 1 and 15 spp. respectively. All Huerteales poorly known.

十齿花科: Huerteales。双齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿齿。所有的胡尔蒂语都鲜为人知。

[Dirachmaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/rosalesweb.htm#Dirachmaceae): Rosales. *Dirachma* (Horn of Africa): 2 spp. Near Rhamnaceae.

大拉菜科: 蔷薇科。大拉菜(非洲之角) : 2页。近鼠李科。

[Euphroniaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/malpighialesweb.htm#Euphroniaceae): Malpighiales. *Euphronia* (N. South America): 3 spp.

大戟科: 锦葵目。大戟属(南美洲北部) : 3种。

[Fabaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/fabalesweb.htm#Fabaceae): Fabales. *Duparquetia* (tropical West Africa): 1 sp. Near basal in family.

豆科: 豆科。豆科(西非热带) : 1个种。近基部科。

[Geissolomataceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/crossosomatalesweb.htm#Geissolomataceae): Crossosomatales. *Geissoloma* (South Africa): 1 sp.

四棱果科: 克罗索马塔尔。

[Gelsemiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/gentianalesweb.htm#Gelsemiaceae): Gentianales. *Pteleocarpa* (W. Malesia): 1 sp. Distinctly odd.

明胶科: 龙胆目。龙胆目(马来西亚属) : 1种。清楚奇数。

[Geraniaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/geranialesweb.htm#Geraniaceae): Geraniales. *Hypseocharis* (Andean South America): 1-3 spp. Sister to rest of family.

洋葵科: 洋葵目。洋葵目(安第斯南美洲) : 1-3个单株。其余家系的姐妹。

[Gerrardinaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/huertealesweb.htm#Gerrardinaceae): Huerteales. *Gerrardina* (S. and E. Africa): 2 spp.; they look rather different. All Huerteales are poorly known.

老虎菌科: 老虎菌目。老虎菌目(非洲南部和东部) : 2个单位; 它们看起来相当不同。所有老虎菌目都很少为人所知。

[Giseckiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Giseckiaceae): Caryophyllales. *Giseckia* (Africa to E. Asia): 5 spp. Core Caryophyllales.

吉赛克科: 石竹目。吉赛克亚目(非洲到东亚) : 5个分支。石竹目。

[Goupiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/malpighialesweb.htm#Goupiaceae): Malpighiales. *Goupia* (Central and N.E. South America): 2 spp. Probably sister to Violaceae.

狗牙蕨科: 狗牙蕨目。狗牙蕨属(南美洲中部和东北部) : 2株。可能是紫堇科的姐妹。

[Griseliniaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/apialesweb.htm#Griseliniaceae): Apiales. *Griselinia* (New Zealand and S. South America): 6 spp.

灰树科: 伞形目。灰树属(新西兰和南美洲) : 6个。

[Grubbiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/cornalesweb.htm#Grubbiaceae): Cornales. *Grubbia* (South Africa, the Cape): 3 sp.

不齿蕨科: 山茱萸目。不齿蕨(南非，好望角) : 3个孢子。

[Guamatelaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/crossosomatalesweb.htm#Guamatelaceae): Crossosomatales. *Guamatela* (Guatemala): 1 sp.

瓜果木科: 杂交目。瓜果木属(危地马拉) : 1种。

[Huaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/oxalidalesweb.htm#Huaceae): Oxalidales. *Afrostyrax*, *Hua* (both tropical W. Africa): 1 and 2 spp. respectively. Perhaps sister all other Oxalidales.

花科: 草酸目。非洲菊科，花科(都是热带的非洲西部) : 分别为1和2。也许是其他草酸目的姊妹。

[Icacinaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/icacinalesweb.html#Icacinaceae): Icacinales. Includes *Casimirella* (Paraguay, 1 sp.), *Cassinopsis* (Africa, Madagascar, 6 spp.), *Hosiea* (China, Japan, 2 spp.), *Mappia* (tropical America, 5 spp.), *Merrillodendron* (Philippines, etc., 1 sp.), *Nothapodytes* (East Asia to Malesia, 4 spp.), *Sarcostigma* (S.E. Asia, W. Malesia, 2 spp.). Basically the whole family...

凤眼莲科: 凤眼莲目。包括 Casimirella (巴拉圭，1 sp.) ，Cassinopsis (非洲，马达加斯加，6 spp.) ，Hosiea (中国，日本，2 spp.) ，mapia (热带美洲，5 spp.) ，merrilodendron (菲律宾等，1 sp.) ，apodytes (东亚至 Malesia，4 spp.) ，sarcostim (东亚，w. Malesia，2 spp.)。基本上全家人..。

[Kewaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Kewaceae): Caryophyllales. *Kewa* (ex *Hypertelis*) (Africa, Saint Helena): 8 spp. Near Aizoaceae, core Caryophyllales.

Kewaceae: 石竹目。 Kewa (非洲，圣赫勒拿) : 8个孢子。靠近 Aizoaceae，石竹目核心。

[Lacistemataceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/malpighialesweb.htm#Lacistemataceae): Malpighiales. *Lacistema*, *Lozania* (both Central and South America): 11 and 3 spp. respectively. Sister to Salicaceae.

马齿蕨科: 马齿蕨目。马齿蕨属，罗扎尼亚(中美洲和南美洲) : 分别为11和3种。 Salicaceae 的姐妹。

[Leycthidaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/ericalesweb.htm#Leycthidaceae): Ericales. *Foetidia* (centred on Madagascar): 17 spp. Napoleonoideae, sister to rest of family - *Crateranthus*, *Napoleona* (both tropical West Africa): 3 and 8 spp. respectively.

赖草科: 杜鹃花目。Foetidia (以马达加斯加为中心) : 17 spp。拿破仑亚科，其余家族的姐妹-Crateranthus，拿破仑亚科(均为西非热带地区) : 分别为3个和8个。

[Lepidobotryaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/celastralesweb.html#Lepidobotryaceae): Celastrales. *Lepidobotrys* (tropical W. Africa), *Ruptiliocarpon* (C. America, W. South America): 1 and 1 spp. respectively. Sister to Celastraceae s.l.

洋酢浆草科: 卫矛。热带非洲西部的 Lepidobotrys，南美洲西部的 ruptiocarpon 分别为1和1。卫矛科的姐妹。

[Limeaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Limeaceae): Caryophyllales. *Limeum* (Africa to Pakistan, esp. South Africa), *Macarthuria* (S.E./S.W. Australia): 26 and 10 spp. respectively. Clade along spine of core Caryophyllales.

石灰科: 石竹目。(从非洲到巴基斯坦，特别是巴基斯坦)。南非) ，Macarthuria (s.e./s.w. 澳大利亚) : 26和10。石竹目核心植物沿刺的分支。

[Lophiocarpaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Lophiocarpaceae): Caryophyllales. *Lophiocarpus* (South Africa), *Corbichonia* (Africa to Asia): 4 and 2 spp. respectively. Sister to speciose clade in core Caryophyllales.

石竹科: 石竹目。南非松果属(Lophiocarpus) ，非洲松果属(Corbichonia) ，亚洲松果属(Corbichonia) ，分别为4个和2个。石竹目核心植物特异分支的姐妹。

[Lophopyxidaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/malpighialesweb.htm#Lophopyxidaceae): Malpighiales. *Lophopyxis* (Malesia to W. Pacific): 1 sp.

[Mayacaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/poalesweb.htm#Mayacaceae): Poales. *Mayaca* (West Africa, tropical America): 4 spp.

Mayacaceae: 山姜目。 Mayaca (西非，热带美洲) : 4 spp。

[Metteniusaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/metteniusalesweb.html#Metteniusaceae): Metteniusales. Includes *Apodytes* (Old World tropics, 15 spp.), *Calatola* (Mexico to Ecuador, 7 spp.), *Dendrobangia* (tropical South America, 2 spp.), *Emmotum* (tropical South America, 12 spp.), *Metteniusa* (Costa Rica to NW South America, 7 spp.), *Platea* (Malesia, 5 spp.), *Rhaphiostylis* (tropical W. Africa, 6 spp.). Again, basically the whole family.

金钱蕨科: 金钱蕨目。包括远足(旧大陆热带，15个单位) ，卡拉托拉(墨西哥到厄瓜多尔，7个单位) ，树木(热带南美洲，2个单位) ，Emmotum (热带南美洲，12个单位) ，Metteniusa (哥斯达黎加到南美洲西北部，7个单位) ，Platea (马里西亚，5个单位) ，rhiphiostylis (热带西非，6个单位)。再说一遍，基本上是全家人。

[Microteaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Microteaceae): Caryophyllales. *Microtea* (Central and South America, Antilles): 9 spp. Perhaps sister to all other core Caryophyllales minus Macarthuriaceae.

小叶藓科: 石竹目。小叶藓科(中南美洲，安的列斯群岛) : 9个小叶藓科。也许是所有其他核心石竹目的姐妹，减去马卡拉瑟科。

[Montiniaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/solanalesweb.htm#Montiniaceae): Solanales. *Grevea* (E. Africa, Madagascar), *Kaliphora* (Madagascar), *Montinia* (S. Africa): 3, 1, and 1 spp. respectively.

蒙替尼科: 茄属。非洲，马达加斯加) ，马达加斯加) ，蒙替尼亚(非洲南部) : 分别为3,1和1。

[Muntingiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/malvalesweb.htm#Muntingiaceae): Malvales. *Dicraspidia* (Central to N.W. South America), *Muntingia* (tropical America, somewhat known): 1 and 1 sp. respectively. *Neotessmannia* (Peru): 1 sp. Does this belong?

芒廷蕨科: 苹果属。迪卡斯皮迪亚(南美洲中部至西北部) ，芒廷贾(热带美洲，多少有些名气) : 分别为1和1个。秘鲁: 1 sp。这个属于这里吗？

[Neuradaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/malvalesweb.htm#Neuradaceae): Malvales. *Grielium* (South Africa), *Neurada* (E. Mediterranean to India), *Neuradopsis* (S.W. Africa): 5, 1 and 3 spp. respectively. ?Sister to all other Malvales.

神经突科: Malvales。Grielium (南非) ，Neurada (东地中海到印度) ，Neuradopsis (南非) : 分别为5,1和3。？是所有其他 Malvales 人的姐妹。

[Nitrariaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/sapindalesweb.htm#Nitrariaceae): Sapindales. *Nitraria* (Mediterranean to C. Asia, S. North America), *Peganum*, *Tetradiclis* (both E. Europe to C. Asia): 12, 6 and 1 spp. respectively.

白刺科: 无患子目。白刺(地中海到亚洲，北美洲南部) ，骆驼蓬，四裂蕨(都是欧洲到亚洲东部)分别为12,6和1个。

[Nyctaginaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Caribeeae): Caryophyllales. *Caribea litoralis* (Cuba). Sister to rest of family.

Nyctaginaceae: 石竹目。斜纹石竹目(古巴)。家族其余成员的姐妹。

[Oncothecaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/oncothecalesweb.htm#Oncothecaceae): Icacinales. *Oncotheca* (New Caledonia): 2 spp. Sister to all other core asterids.

喜鹊科: Icacinales。喜鹊科(新喀里多尼亚) : 2 spp. 所有其他核心星群的姐妹。

[Orobanchaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/lamialesweb.htm#Orobanchaceae): Lamiales. *Rehmannia* (East Asia), *Trianeophora* (EastAsia): 6 and 3 spp. respectively. Sister to rest of family.

列当科: 列当目。地黄属(东亚) ，列当目(东亚) : 分别为6和3个。是其余家系的姐妹。

[Passifloraceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/malpighialesweb.html#Pibirioideae): Malpighiales. *Pibiria* (Guyana): 1 sp. Sister to Turneroideae.

西番莲科: Malpighiales. Pibiria (圭亚那) : 1 sp. Turneroideae 的姊妹。

[Paracryphiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/Paracryphiales.html#Paracryphiaceae): Paracryphiales. *Paracryphia* (New Caledonia), *Quintinia* (Philippines to New Zealand), *Sphenostemon* (Celebes to N.E. Australia and New Caledonia); 1, 25, and 10 spp. respectively. Sister to Apiales.

伞形目: 伞形目。Paraciphia (新喀里多尼亚) ，Quintinia (菲律宾到新西兰) ，Sphenostemon (西里伯斯到 N.E. Australia 和新喀里多尼亚) ，分别为1,25和10 spp。Apiales 的姐妹。

[Pennantiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/apialesweb.htm#Pennantiaceae): Apiales. *Pennantia* (E. Australia to New Zealand): 4 spp. Sister to all other Apiales.

宾夕法尼亚科: 伞形目。 Pennantia -LRB- E. Australia 至新西兰) : 4个。

[Pentadiplandraceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/brassicalesweb.htm#Pentadiplandraceae): Brassicales. *Pentadiplandra* (tropical W. Africa): 1 sp. Core Brassicales.

瘤药树科属: 芸苔目。五倍木兰属(热带非洲 w。) : 1个。芸苔目核心。

[Pentaphragmataceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Pentaphragmataceae): Asterales. *Pentaphragma* (S.E. Asia-Malesia): 30 spp. Sister to major clade in order.

五膜草科: Asterales. Pentaphragma (s.e. Asia-Malesia) : 30 spp. 依次为 major clade 的姐妹。

[Peridiscaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/saxifragalesweb.htm#Peridiscaceae): Saxifragales. *Medusandra*, *Soyauxia* (both tropical W. Africa), *Peridiscus* (Amazonia), *Whittonia* (N. South America): 2, 7, 1, and 1 spp. respectively. Sister to all other Saxifragales.

橄榄科: 虎耳草属。分别为2、7、1和1株。她是所有 Saxifragales 人的姐妹。

[Petenaeaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/huertealesweb.htm#Petenaeaceae): Huerteales. *Petenaea* (C. America): 1 sp. Order poorly known.

石首藓科: 石首藓目。石首藓属(美洲石首藓属) : 1纲。

[Phellinaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Phellinaceae): Asterales. *Phelline* (New Caledonia): 12 spp.

山茱萸科: 海星目。山茱萸属(新喀里多尼亚) : 12种。

[Phyllonomaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/aquifolialesweb2.htm#Phyllonomaceae): Aquifoliales. *Phyllonoma* (Mexico to W. South America): 4 spp.

拟叶菌科: 冬青目。拟叶菌(墨西哥至南美洲西部) : 4个。

[Picramniaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/picramnialesweb.html#Picramniaceae): Picramniales. *Alvaradoa* (Florida, Central America, Bahama, esp. the Greater Antilles, Bolivia to Argentina), *Nothotalisia* (Panama and N.W. South America), *Picramnia* (Florida, Central and South America): 5, 3, and 41 spp. respectively. Along spine of malvids.

胡萝卜科: 胡萝卜目。阿尔瓦拉多亚(佛罗里达州，中美洲，Bahama，尤其是。大安的列斯群岛，玻利维亚到阿根廷) ，Nothotalisia (巴拿马和西南美洲) ，Picramnia (佛罗里达，中美洲和南美洲)分别为5,3和41个单位。沿着海葵的脊柱。

[Poaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/poalesweb.htm#Poaceae): Poales. Pharoideae: *Leptaspis* (Old World tropics), *Pharus* (New World, Florida to Argentina): 4 and 8 spp. respectively. Puelioideae: *Guaduella*, *Puelia* (both tropical W. Africa): 6 and 5 spp. respectively. Clades along basal spine of family.

禾本科: 禾本科。法罗亚科: 东半球热带地区，佛罗里达至阿根廷地区，分别为4和8。南亚科: Guaduella，Puelia (均为热带非洲西部) ，分别为6和5个。沿着科的基部脊的分支。

[Physenaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Physenaceae): Caryophyllales. *Physena* (Madagascar): 2 spp. One family of two in clade sister to core Caryophyllales, see also Asteropeiaceae.

植物门蕨科: 石竹目。植物门蕨目(马达加斯加) : 2个门蕨属。属于核心石竹目的姐妹分支中的一个两个科。

[Plocospermataceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/lamialesweb.htm#Plocospermataceae): Lamiales. *Plocospermum* (Central America): 1 sp. Sister to all other Lamiales.

环生籽科: Lamiales. Plocospermum (中美洲) : 1 sp. . 所有其他 Lamiales 的姐妹。

[Picrodendraceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/malpighialesweb.htm#Picrodendraceae): Malpighiales. *Podocalyx* (Amazonian South America): 1 sp. Sister to rest of family.

苦木科: 麦芽目。山药属(南美洲亚马逊河流域) : 1属。其余家系的姐妹。

[Portulacaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Portulacaceae): Caryophyllales. *Portulaca* (pan(sub)tropical): 40-100 spp. Once-removed from sister to Cactaceae.

马齿苋科: 石竹目。马齿苋(亚热带) : 40-100株。曾从仙人掌科的姐妹植物中分离出来。

[Primulaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/ericalesweb.htm#Primulaceae): Ericales. *Maesa* (Old World Tropics): 160 spp. Sister to rest of family.

报春花科: 杜鹃花科。梅萨(旧大陆热带) : 160株。其余科的姐妹。

[Quillajaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/fabalesweb.htm#Quillajaceae): Fabales. *Quillaja* (temperate South America): ca 3 spp.

奎拉加科: 豆科。奎拉加(南美洲温带) : 约3个 spp。

[Resedaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/brassicalesweb.htm#Resedaceae): *Forchhammeria* (S.W. North America), *Stixis* (E. Himalayas to W. Malesia), *Neothorelia* (Laos), *Tirania* (Vietnam): 10, 7, 1 and 1 spp. respectively. Also *Borthwickia* (S.W. Yunnan, China, and adjacent Burma): 1 sp.

树脂科: 北美洲胡枝蕨属，喜马拉雅山至马里西亚胡枝蕨属，老挝胡枝蕨属，越南地拉那蕨属，分别为10,7,1和1株。还有博斯维奇亚(中国云南西南部及邻近的缅甸) : 1 sp。

[Rhizophoraceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/malpighialesweb.htm#Rhizophoraceae): Malpighiales. *Paradrypetes* (tropical South America): 2 spp. Very odd genus.

根蕨科: 锦葵目。热带南美洲: 2个孢子。非常奇怪的属。

[Rousseaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asteralesweb.htm#Rousseaceae): Asterales. One clade includes *Roussea* (Mauritius): 1 sp. The other clade includes *Abrophyllum* (E. Australia), *Carpodetus* (New Guinea to New Zealand), *Cuttsia* (E. Australia): 1, 2, and 1 spp. respectively. Sister to Campanulaceae.

罗苏科: 菊目。其中一个支系包括 rousea (毛里求斯) : 1 sp。另一支系分别为棕叶(澳大利亚)、新几内亚至新西兰)、墨枝(澳大利亚) : 1、2和1。桔梗科的姐妹。

[Sapindaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/sapindalesweb.htm#Sapindaceae): Sapindales. *Xanthoceras* (China): 1 sp. Possibly sister to rest of family

无患子科: 无患子目。文冠果属(中国) : 1种。可能是其余科的姐妹

[Sarcobataceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Sarcobataceae): Caryophyllales. *Sarcobatus* (S.W. North America): 2 spp. Core Caryophyllales, position unclear.

肉豆蔻科: 石竹目。肉豆蔻目(北美西南部) : 2个分支。石竹目核心目，位置不明。

[Setchellanthaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/brassicalesweb.htm#Setchellanthaceae): Brassicales. *Setchellanthus* (S.W. U.S.A., Mexico): 1 sp. Along spine of Brassicales.

夷白花菜科: Brassicales. Setchellanthus (s.w. u.s.a. ，Mexico) : 1 sp. 沿着 Brassicales 的脊柱。

[Simmondsiaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Simmondsiaceae): Caryophyllales. *Simmondsia* (S.W. U.S.A., Mexico): 1 sp. Along spine just below core Caryophyllales.

Simmondsia -LRB- S.W. U.S.A.) : 1 sp. 沿着刚好在石竹目核心下面的脊柱。

[Sladeniaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/ericalesweb.htm#Sladeniaceae): Ericales. *Ficalhoa* (East Africa), *Sladenia* (S. E. Asia): 1 and ?2 spp. respectively.

斯拉德尼亚科: 杜鹃花科，东非菲卡尔霍亚科，东亚斯拉德尼亚科: 分别为1和2。

[Stegnospermataceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/caryophyllalesweb.htm#Stegnospermataceae): Caryophyllales. *Stegnospermum* (Central America, Antilles): 3 spp. Along spine of core Caryophyllales.

暗种子科: 石竹目。暗种子目(中美洲，安的列斯群岛) : 3个 spp. 沿着石竹目核心的脊柱。

[Surianaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/fabalesweb.htm#Surianaceae): Fabales. *Cadelia* (N.E. Australia), *Guilfoylia* (E. Australia), *Recchia* (Mexico), *Stylobasium* (W. and N. Australia), *Suriana* (pantropical, a little known): 1, 1, 3, 2 and 1 spp. respectively. Position in order unclear.

苏伦亚科: 法贝目。卡德利亚(澳大利亚东北部)、吉尔福利亚(澳大利亚东部)、雷奇亚(墨西哥)、柱花草(西澳大利亚和北澳大利亚)、苏里亚纳(一个鲜为人知的泛热带) : 分别为1、1、3、2和1。位置依次不明。

[Tapisciaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/huertealesweb.htm#Tapisciaceae): Huerteales. *Huertea* (Central and South America), *Tapiscia* (E. Asia): 4 and 1 spp. respectively. Whole order poorly known

Tapisciaceae: 花叶目。花叶目(中美洲和南美洲) ，花叶目(东亚) : 分别为4和1。全目知之甚少

[Tetracarpaeaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/saxifragalesweb.htm#Tetracarpaeaceae): Saxifragales. *Tetracarpaea* (Tasmania): 1 sp.

四果木科: 虎耳草。四环素(塔斯马尼亚) : 1 sp。

[Tetrachondraceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/lamialesweb.htm#Tetrachondraceae): Lamiales. *Polypremum* (New World), *Tetrachondra* (New Zealand, Chile): 1 and 2 spp. respectively. Sister to very speciose monosymmetric Core Lamiales.

四粉草科: Lamiales。多前菊(新大陆) ，四色苔(新西兰，智利) : 1和2分别。姐妹到非常特殊的单对称核心 Lamiales。

[Ticodendraceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/fagalesweb.htm#Ticodendraceae): Fagales. *Ticodendron* (Central America): 1 sp.

毛蕨科: 壳斗目。毛蕨属(中美洲) : 1属。

[Torricelliaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/apialesweb.htm#Torricelliaceae): Apiales. *Aralidium* (W. Malesia), *Melanophylla* (Madagascar), *Torricellia* (Southeast Asia): 1, 7, and 2 spp. respectively. Sister to all Apiales minus Pennantiaceae.

托利加科: 伞形目。Aralidium (W.Malesia) ，Melanophylla (Madagascar) ，Torricellia (Southeast Asia) : 1,7,2 spp.妹妹以所有的伞形目减去金丝桃科。

[Vahliaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/solanalesweb.htm#Vahliaceae): unplaced asterid I. *Vahlia* (Africa, Madagascar, Indian subcontinent): 8 spp.

非洲，马达加斯加，印度次大陆。

[Wellstediaceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/boraginalesweb.htm#Wellstediaceae): Boraginales. *Wellstedia* (N.E. Africa, South West Africa): 6 spp. Sister to Boraginaceae.

紫草科: 紫草目。 Wellstedia -LRB- N.E. Africa，西南非) : 6 spp. 紫草科姊妹。

[Xeronemataceae](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/asparagalesweb.htm#Xeronemataceae): Asparagales. *Xeronema* (New Zealand, New Caledonia): 1 sp. Along spine of Asparagales.

门冬酰胺科: 门冬酰胺目。门冬酰胺目(新西兰，新喀里多尼亚) : 1 sp. 沿 Asparagales 脊。

**ON THE ORGANIZATION AND DESIGN OF THE SITE**
[Back to Top](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/introductionnew.htm#top)

网站的组织及设计[返回页首]

This website is best viewed using the most recent version of your preferred internet browser. You can tell when each page was last updated if you look at the top of each page, or, for the individual order pages, immediately below mention of the order or other major clade first mentioned on that page - thus on the Arecales page the update indication is below the characterization of the commelinid group.

本网站最好使用最新版本的浏览器浏览。如果你看到每一页的顶部，或者是单个订单页面，你可以知道每一页上一次更新的时间，或者在该页面上第一次提到的订单或其他主要的分支的下面，因此在槟榔石页面上，更新指示在商标组的角色塑造下面。

The **left pane** is designed as a quick entry into different parts of the seed plant phylogeny. The default pane includes a reference list of accepted orders as well as a listing of abbreviations, etc., used in the body of the text. There are also direct links to the developing essays on seed plant evolution and angiosperm evolution and diversification. This left pane can be replaced by a list of the main characters that are described in detail elsewhere - see the "Characters" option in the top pane of the website.

左边的窗格设计为快速进入种子植物系统发育的不同部分。默认窗格包括已接受订单的参考列表以及文本正文中使用的缩写等的列表。种子植物进化、被子植物进化和多样化的发展论文也有直接的联系。这个左窗格可以替换为在其他地方详细描述的主要字符列表-请参阅网站顶部窗格中的“字符”选项。

The **top pane** is designed as a menu:

顶部窗格设计为一个菜单:

- [Home](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/welcome.html) will always return the user to this page.

- 主页总是将用户返回到此页面。

- [Tree](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/treeapweb2map.html) gets you to the Main Tree that displays a phylogeny of the orders. Clicking once on the name of a terminal taxon will take you to a characterization of that taxon. Clicking on a node will take you to that particular node. Clicking on one of the tree icons next to an ordinal name will usually take you a tree showing relationships within that order. Not all orders have such icons; some are too small. Clicking on "Unplaced Taxa" will send the user to those few families and genera that lack any convincing evidence as to their likely immediate relationships.

- Tree 将您带到主树，该主树显示各命令的系统发展史。点击一下终端分类单元的名称，你就会找到该分类单元的一个角色塑造。单击一个节点将把您带到该特定的节点。单击序号名旁边的一个树图标，通常会得到一个显示该顺序内关系的树。不是所有的订单都有这样的图标，有些太小了。点击“未放置的分类群”将把用户发送到那些缺乏任何令人信服的证据可能的直接关系的少数科和属。

- [Orders](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/synonymyorders.html) provides an alphabetical listing of all accepted ordinal names and also all synonyms. Clicking on a letter at the top of the page will take you to the beginning of names that start with that particular letter.

- 按字母顺序提供所有接受的序号名称和所有同义词的一个字母表。点击页面顶部的一个字母，你会看到以这个字母开头的名字的开头。

- [Families](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/synonymyfamilies.html) is an alphabetical listing of all accepted family names and their synonyms. Clicking on a letter at the top of the page will take you to the beginning of names that start with that particular letter. Clicking on a link to a family will take you to its characterization.

- 家庭是一个按字母顺序排列的所有接受的家庭名称及其同义词。点击页面顶部的一个字母，你会看到以这个字母开头的名字的开头。点击一个家庭的链接，你就会进入这个家庭的角色塑造。

- [Characters](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/characters.htm) provides a textual description of characters used to support the recognition and/or monophyly of a particular taxon. General references that are important sources of data for this project are also included. At the beginning of this page is a notice "click here"; this will display a list of the major characters included in the left pane. One can return to the **Orders** list by choosing the option "Back to Orders" at the beginning of the character list.

- 字符提供字符的文本描述，用于支持特定分类单元的识别和/或单系统。还包括作为该项目重要数据来源的一般引用。在这个页面的开头是一个通知“单击此处”; 这将显示包含在左窗格中的主要字符的列表。您可以通过在字符列表的开头选择“ Back to Orders”选项返回到“ Orders”列表。

- [References](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/referencesa_d.html) provide an alphabetical listing of the references cited; it has been broken down into six interlinked pages for ease of loading. Clicking on a letter at the top or the bottom of the page will take you to the part of the reference list where surnames with that letter begin. Articles with two authors are listed alphabetically by name of second author and then by date, articles with three or more authors are cited last (e.g. as "Chase [et al. 1993]") and are listed by date. You can also search on individual authors' names.

- 参考资料按字母顺序列出所引用的参考资料; 为了便于加载，已将参考资料分成六个相互关联的页面。点击页面顶部或底部的一个字母，你就会进入参考列表中姓氏以字母开头的部分。有两位作者的文章按第二位作者姓名字母顺序排列，然后按日期排列，最后引用有三位或三位以上作者的文章(例如“ Chase [等人，1993]”) ，并按日期排列。你也可以搜索个别作者的名字。

- ["Search"](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/search.html) takes you to a page where you may enter keywords or terms that you are interested in finding within the Angiosperm Phylogeny Website. The search engine is unfortunately not designed to search for wildcards, so if your search is not successful, please try variations of your search terms. [Para. to be changed.]

- “搜索”带你到一个页面，你可以输入关键字或术语，你感兴趣的发现在被子植物系统发展网站。不幸的是，这个搜索引擎不是设计来搜索通配符的，所以如果你的搜索不成功，请尝试你的搜索词的变化。第一段。[被改变]

- [Links](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/links.html) lists some other websites or web utilities that are relevant to general classification, floras (a few), image resources, and phylogeny. These listings are very incomplete. There are also some links to other websites in the Bibliography and on individual ordinal pages.

- 链接列出一些其他网站或网络公用事业是相关的一般分类，植物区系(一些) ，图像资源，和系统发展。这些列表是非常不完整的。还有一些链接到其他网站的书目和单独的序号页面。

- The [Glossary](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/glossarya_h.html#Glossary) is made up of three separate pages. Clicking on a letter at the top or the bottom of the page will take you to th first definition starting with that particular letter. Within the Glossary, there are cross references to characters at the same level. Thus when reading the definition of paracytic stomata, you will find direct links to other types of stomata such as anomocytic, cyclocytic, etc. There are also links to definitions at other levels, e.g. to stomata in general, where the basic features of stomata are described, and also to variants of individual stomatal types such as brachyparacytic stomata. We have also built in some synonymy, e.g., Rubiaceous stomata are a synonym of paracytic stomata.

- 《词汇》共有三页。点击页面顶部或底部的一个字母，你会看到第一个定义，从这个特定的字母开始。在词汇表中，对同一级别的字符有交叉引用。因此，当你阅读平列气孔的定义时，你会发现它与其他类型的气孔有直接的联系，例如无规则气孔、细胞性气孔等。还有其他级别的定义的链接，例如描述气孔基本特征的一般气孔类型，以及单个气孔类型的变体，例如短平列气孔类型。我们还建立了一些同义词，例如，茜草属植物的气孔是平列气孔的同义词。

The names of the images of plants may not be up to date - sorry. We did not chose the most spectacular photographs we could find, rather, I tried to select those that showed at least some features on the plant that help characterize the group to which it belongs. All photographs are copyrighted as is evident from the characterizations or the images or the external websites themselves. For photographs of individual species and genera, or simply for more images of families, use Google, but beware of the identifications there!

植物图片的名称可能不是最新的-对不起。我们没有选择我们能找到的最壮观的照片，相反，我试图选择那些至少显示了植物的一些特征，有助于描述它所属的种群。所有的照片都是有版权的，因为从人物刻画、图片或者外部网站本身就可以看出来。对于单个物种和属的照片，或者仅仅是更多的科的照片，可以使用谷歌，但要注意那里的标识！

**Website Design:** The html code and javascript code for the website were originally generated by hand by Hilary Davis and by using HomeSite © Allaire/Macromedia Corp., and problems dealt with as they appeared. Everything was migrated to [Adobe Dreamweaver](http://www.adobe.com/products/dreamweaver.html) in March 2015, and a new version of this was installed in November 2019. The general design is a three frame set-up. The top frame contains the "menu," the side frame contains the "quick reference" lists of orders, characters, etc.. The middle frame is the most dynamic and is where most of the pages are displayed. The trees were created by generating a raw dataset in MacClade and drawing the trees in the tree editing window. The tree files were then accessed in PAUP and saved as .pict files to facilitate use in Adobe Illustrator. After polishing the tree images in Illustrator, each tree was saved as a .gif file. Each tree image was made into an image map using a tool in HomeSite, which allows you to select any part of the image (treated as coordinates) and assign a link for those particular coordinates to any place within the website or to any other current website. Note that a number of trees are out of date, so be careful when using them; relationships in the text are more reliable.

网站设计: 网站的 html 代码和 javascript 代码最初是由 Hilary Davis 和 HomeSite Allaire/Macromedia corp. 手工生成的，出现问题时就会处理。在2015年3月，所有的东西都被移植到了 Adobe Dreamweaver，并且在2019年11月安装了一个新版本。总体设计为三框架结构。顶部框架包含“菜单”，侧面框架包含“快速参考”的订单列表，字符等。中间的框架是最有活力的，也是大多数页面显示的地方。这些树是通过在 macdade 中生成一个原始数据集并在树编辑窗口中绘制树来创建的。然后在 PAUP 中访问树文件并将其保存为。培训及通讯科技档案，方便 Adobe Illustrator 使用。在 Illustrator 中抛光树形图之后，每棵树都被保存为一个。Gif 文件。每张树图都是使用 HomeSite 中的一个工具制作成图像地图的，它允许你选择图像的任何部分(作为坐标处理) ，并为这些特定的坐标分配一个链接到网站内的任何地方或任何其他当前的网站。请注意，许多树已经过时，因此在使用它们时要小心; 文本中的关系更可靠。

**ON THE INTERPRETATION OF THE TREES, TEXT, ABBREVIATIONS, ETC.**
[Back to Top](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/introductionnew.htm#top)

关于树木、文字、缩写等的解释[返回页首]

In the trees in this site I have emphasized mostly nodes with substantial support (e.g. ³80% bootstrap support) that appear after analysis of data from more than one gene; posterior probabilities for a particular node are usually substantially higher than its bootstrap or jacknife values. In a few cases I have been somewhat less cautious, but I have always tried to make it clear where I am treading on thin ice. There are references (not exhaustive) to papers giving support for the relationships suggested here, and these papers may have more resolved trees than those shown, albeit details of these topologies may on occasion have little support. Chase et al (1993, 2000a), Olmstead et al. (1992, 1993, 2000), Olmstead and Graham (2000a, b), Savolainen et al. (2000a, b), D. Soltis et al. (1997, 1998, 2000, 2003, 2005b, 2017), P. Soltis et al. (2000), B. Bremer et al. (2002), Hilu et al. (2003), Jansen et al. (2007), Saarela et al. (2007), Moore et al. (2007, 2010), etc., are invaluable sources for the developing big picture of angiosperm relationships.

在这个站点的树中，我强调了大多数节点都有实质性的支持(例如380% bootstrap 支持) ，这些节点在分析了来自多个基因的数据之后才出现; 一个特定节点的后验概率通常大大高于它的 bootstrap 或 jacknife 值。在一些情况下，我没有那么谨慎，但我总是试图弄清楚自己在哪里如履薄冰。这里有一些参考文献(不是详尽无遗的)支持这里所建议的关系，而且这些文献可能比那些显示的文献有更多的解析树，尽管这些拓扑的细节有时可能没有什么支持。蔡斯等人(1993,2000 a) ，奥尔姆斯特德等人(1992,1993,2000) ，奥尔姆斯特德和格雷厄姆(2000 a，b) ，萨沃莱宁等人(2000 a，b) ，d. 索尔蒂斯等人(1997,1998,2000,2003,2005 b，2017) ，p. 索尔蒂斯等人。(2000年),b. Bremer 等人(2002) ，Hilu 等人(2003) ，Jansen 等人(2007) ，Saarela 等人(2007) ，Moore 等人(2007,2010)等。，是被子植物关系发展的重要资料来源。

If one printed out all the trees in this site and stuck them all together, it might seem as if one had some kind of supertree, however, it is clear from the description of my *modus operandi* that these trees are hardly a formal supertree. Readers who are interested in the topology of *the* most parsimonious tree, or relationships suggested by poorly supported nodes, etc., should consult the original literature. [PhyloMatic](http://www.phylodiversity.net/phylomatic) is a another resource to be used.

如果一个人把这个地方的所有树都打印出来，然后把它们粘在一起，看起来就像是有某种超级树，然而，从我的作案手法来看，很明显这些树并不是正式的超级树。对最简约的树的拓扑结构感兴趣的读者，或者对支持不足的节点所建议的关系感兴趣的读者，应该查阅原始文献。PhyloMatic 是另一种要使用的资源。

For an introduction to the interpretation of phylogenetic trees, see Baum and Smith (2012). Krell and Cranston (2004) and Crisp and Cook (2005) and many others have emphasized how careful one must be when interpreting and talking about ladderised trees (see above) in particular and phylogenetic trees in general; the use of the adjective "basal" is especially dangerous (see also D. Soltis et al. 2005b). However, when describing relationships in the context of a branching phylogenetic tree, the use of terms like "high", "low", "basal", etc., to describe aspects of the branching pattern might seem perfectly appropriate, but it is difficult to talk about branching points of a phylogenetic tree; there is no trunk, and no "branch" - one member of a pair of sister clades - can be basal to the other. Although on occasion, I do use the term "basal", this is in the context of a ladderized tree (see above) and refers to the branch in which there has subsequently been less diversification. Thus *Equisetum*, *Amborella*, *Acorus*, *Enkianthus*, *Humbertia*, and many other clades can all be called "basal" from this point of view - but note that this has only the topological connotations I have just mentioned, there is certainly no implication that these taxa lack apomorphies or are "primitive" in any way. Indeed, the terms "primitive" and "advanced" are heavily loaded and I have tried not to use them; "plesiomorphic" and its opposite, "derived" and "apomorphic", are the terms to use when talking about individual characters.

关于系统发育树解释的介绍，见 Baum 和 Smith (2012)。Krell 和 Cranston (2004年)和 Crisp 和 Cook (2005年)以及其他许多人都强调，在解释和讨论阶梯化树(见上文)以及一般的系统发育树时，必须非常小心; 使用形容词“基础”尤其危险(另见 d. Soltis et al. 2005b)。然而，在描述分支系统发生树的上下文中的关系时，使用诸如“高”、“低”、“基底”等术语来描述分支模式的各个方面似乎是完全合适的，但是很难谈论系统发生树的分支点; 没有树干，也没有“分支”——一对姐妹支系中的一个成员——可以相对于另一个基底。虽然有时我确实使用“基础”一词，但这是在梯度化树的上下文中(见上文) ，指的是随后变得不那么多样化的分支。因此，从这个观点来看，木贼属、安博瑞拉属、菖蒲属、钩吻属、 Humbertia 属以及许多其他支系都可以被称为“基础”——但是请注意，这只有我刚才提到的拓扑内涵，当然没有暗示这些分类群缺乏自同构性或者说这些分类群在任何方面都是“原始”的。事实上，“原始”和“先进”这两个术语负担很重，我尽量不去使用它们; “ plesiomorphic”和它的反义词“ derived”和“ apmorphic”是谈论单个字符时使用的术语。

In connection with this ladderisation of the trees, comments on particular nodes - whether subtending dichotomies or polytomies - are to be found on the page where the first branch (reading from left to right) at that node is mentioned, and there are cross-links between pages in important cases. Thus comments on the relationships of the magnoliid clade, which involves discussion of the relationships between Chloranthales, monocots, Ceratophyllaceae and eudicots as well, are to be found on the [Chloranthales](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/chloranthalesweb.htm#ChltoRest) page alone, however, the discussion there is cross-linked to the other pages. However, comments on relationships within the magnoliid group itself are to be found on the [Magnoliales](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/magnolialesweb.htm#Maglaucanpip) page alone.

关于树木的阶梯化，特定节点上的注释——无论是二分法还是多分法——都可以在提到该节点的第一个分支(从左向右阅读)的页面上找到，而且在重要情况下，页面之间存在交叉链接。因此，关于木兰科植物之间亲缘关系的讨论，也包括 Chloranthales、单子叶植物、金盏花科植物和真皮植物之间亲缘关系的讨论，仅见于金兰目页面，而与其他页面的讨论有交叉关联。然而，关于玉兰科植物组内部关系的评论仅在玉兰科植物页面上可以找到。

The information at the beginning of each page is to be read as if you were following along from the base of the embryophyte tree to the branch in which you are interested. Thus each page starts off with a characterisation of the common ancestor of all embryophytes followed by characterisations of all nodes leading up to your branch. Of course, features mentioned more basally in the tree (earlier on that page) may change, perhaps even reverse. Thus at the node [AUSTROBAILEYALES [CHLORANTHALES + MAGNOLIIDS] [MONOCOTS [CERATOPHYLLALES + EUDICOTS] you will find "ethereal oils +" - this part of the tree seems to be where that feature evolved. However, the apomorphies of [CERATOPHYLLALES + EUDICOTS] and of all monocots minus Acorales include "ethereal oils 0". Ethereal oils have also subsequently been reacquired several times, as in Zingiberaceae and within Lamiaceae.

每一页开头的信息应该被阅读，就好像你从胚胎植物树的基部一直到你感兴趣的分枝一样。因此，每一页都以所有胚胎植物的共同祖先的角色塑造开始，然后是通向你的分支的所有节点的特征。当然，树中提到的更基本的特性(在该页面的前面)可能会发生变化，甚至可能出现相反的情况。因此，在木兰藤目[绿兰目 + 木兰科][单子叶植物[角叶目 + 真皮植物]节点处，你会发现“虚无的植物油 +”——树的这一部分似乎就是这种特征演化的地方。然而，[ ceratophylales + EUDICOTS ]和所有单子叶植物减 Acorales 的近似模式包括“空灵油0”。如 Zingiberaceae 和唇形科植物中的精油后来也被重新获得过几次。

The families and orders are those recognized by the Angiosperm Phylogeny Group (A.P.G. IV 2016), any differences reflecting subsequent work (see individual pages). Families are grouped within orders as far as possible according to their phylogenetic relationships. Trees showing relationships within many orders and a few of the larger families are included; they may have been cobbled together from more than one study, and I may indicate the level of support for the nodes on the trees. Subfamilies or tribes are numbered sequentially within each family. Although their characterisations may be only imperfectly worked out, they help clarify which characters really are potential family-level apomorphies and which characterise only parts of the family, speciose though those parts may be. The importance of having infra-familial variation pegged to its correct level is evident in, for example, Annonaceae, Convolvulaceae and Fabaceae. Paraphyletic groups are clearly flagged as being such, e.g. "Caesalpinioideae" (paraphyletic) vs Faboideae (monophyletic) - although there is now a particular circumscription of Caesalpinioideae which is monophyletic that can be used (see the Legume Phylogeny Working Group 2017). Further details of relationships, etc., can be found in the papers cited, which should always be consulted.

家庭和命令是那些被被子植物种系发生学组认可的(a.p.g. IV 2016) ，任何反映后续工作的差异(见单页)。科尽可能根据它们的系统发育关系按顺序分组。树木显示了许多序列中的关系和一些较大的家族被包括在内; 他们可能是从一个以上的研究中拼凑起来的，我可以指出对树木上的节点的支持程度。子族或部落在每个族内按顺序编号。虽然他们的特点可能只是不完美的工作，他们有助于澄清哪些字符真的是潜在的家庭级别的共同点，哪些只是家庭的部分特征，虽然这些部分可能是特殊的。在番荔枝科、旋花科和豆科植物中，家系内变异与正确水平挂钩的重要性是显而易见的。近海属的种群被清楚地标记为这样，例如“苏木亚科”(近海属) vs Faboideae (单系)-尽管现在有一个特殊的单系苏木亚科的界限可以使用(见豆科系统发育学工作组2017)。进一步的关系细节，等等，可以在引用的文件中找到，应该总是参考。

For the authorities of the names of subfamilies, families, orders, etc., I have relied largely on Reveal's listings ([Reveal 2001](javascript:showImage('http://www.plantsystematics.org/reveal/pbio/WWW/supragen.html',600,500)) onwards), Hoogland and Reveal (2005) and Thorne (with Reveal) (2007). However, the authors of some names as given here may be incorrect since bibliographic work that affects the names of authorities proceeds apace. Synonymy is as complete as I can get it at the familial level and above.

我主要依靠 Reveal 的列表(Reveal 2001年以后)、 Hoogland 和 Reveal (2005年)和 Thorne (与 Reveal 合作)(2007年)来掌握亚家族、家族、宗派等的名字。然而，这里给出的一些名字的作者可能是不正确的，因为书目工作会迅速影响当局的名字。在家族层面和以上层面，我已经尽可能完整地获得了同义词。

Features are mentioned in the characterisations roughly following the order in the discussion of the characters on the ["Characters"](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/characters.htm) page. Possible apomorphies are indicated, but it will be abundantly clear that fixing characters to nodes is no easy task. For some characters (an example is leaf ptyxis) there is little easily-accessible basic information and the terms used to describe it in the literature are not used consistently. It is not always recorded in the characterisations, although its coverage is slowly improving; the same is true for the pattern of petiole vasculature, presence of pericyclic fibers in the stem, etc.; I had initially not considered such characters to be particularly useful (and this indeed may be true of petiole anatomy). Gaps in data are often indicated, but for many features confidently included in a characterisation, e.g. micropyle type, it should not be forgotten that this may be known for very few taxa. The contraction P stands for perianth, T for tepals, K for calyx, C for corolla, A for androecium, and G for gynoecium. "#<" means equal to or more than, "<#" means equal to or fewer than. "Many" means that there are more than fifteen or so parts. Parentheses in characterisations of clades above the level of family denote characters that are scattered throughout that clade, being found in several, but not all, terminal taxa but in no obvious pattern. Examples are septal nectaries and cuticle waxes in monocots, N-fixing in part of the eurosid I clade, and iridoids in asterids. Parentheses in characterizations of terminal taxa refer (as in conventional descriptions) to uncommon features. Square brackets enclose explanations or glosses of the feature described. When a generic name is placed in square brackets after mention of a feature, this emphasized that the feature is known from/I know of it from only that one genus. However, square brackets surrounding carpel number means that the carpels are connate, at least as to their ovule-bearing parts. A line under the number of carpels means that the ovary is superior. A fuller list of abbreviations, etc., used may be found under **"Abbreviations"** on the top of the left pane.

在特征描述中，特征的提及大致遵循“字符”页上字符讨论的顺序。可能的逆向营销是表明，但将非常清楚，固定字符的节点是不容易的任务。对于一些字符(例如树叶习惯) ，很少有易于理解的基本信息，而且文献中用来描述它的术语并不一致使用。它并不总是被记录在特征，虽然它的覆盖范围正在缓慢地改善; 同样的情况发生在叶柄的脉管系统，在茎的周环纤维的存在，等等; 我一开始并不认为这些特征特别有用(这可能确实是叶柄解剖学)。数据中的空白经常被指出，但是对于角色塑造中的许多特征，例如珠孔类型，不应该忘记，这可能是为数不多的分类群所知的。收缩 p 代表花被，t 代表花被，k 代表花萼，c 代表花冠，a 代表雄蕊群，g 代表雌蕊群# <”表示等于或多于,”< #”表示等于或少于。“ Many”意思是多于十五个部分。科级以上的分支特征中的括号表示分布在整个分支中的特征，分布在几个但不是全部的终端分类群中，但没有明显的模式。例如单子叶植物中的隔蜜腺和角质层蜡，部分 eurosid i 分支中的 n 固定，星群中的环烯醚萜。在末端分类群的特征描述中的括号指的是不常见的特征(如常规描述)。方括号内包含所描述特性的解释或注释。当一个通用名称在提到一个特征后放在方括号中时，这强调了这个特征是已知的/我只从一个属知道它。然而，心皮数目的方括号表示心皮是合生的，至少对于它们的胚珠生长部分是合生的。心皮数目下的一条线表示子房是上位的。在左侧窗格顶部的“缩写”下面可以找到更全面的缩写列表等。

Following familial and subfamilial characterisations are two figures, the approximate number of accepted genera and species in the group. I mention most genera with 50 or more species and estimate total numbers of species and genera in families; much of this information is taken from Mabberley's excellent *The Plant Book* (Mabberley 2008) and from accounts in Kubitzki (1993 onwards). A list of included genera and their synonyms can usually be found by clicking on "list". Coverage of the synonymy is variable, and keeping up-to-date on new generic names is impossible. In general, the patient user will be able to answer most questions about the authorities of generic names, commonly-used synonyms, etc.. There are also some links to images.

以下的家族和亚家族特征是两个数字，大约数量的公认属和种群。我提到的大多数属有50个或更多的物种，并估算出科的物种和属的总数，这些信息大部分来自 Mabberley 优秀的《植物图书》(Mabberley 2008)和 Kubitzki 的会计(1993年以后)。通过点击“列表”可以找到所包含的属及其同义词的列表。同义词的覆盖范围是可变的，不可能保持对新的通用名称的最新信息。一般来说，患者用户将能够回答有关通用名称、常用同义词等权威的大多数问题。还有一些图片的链接。

General distribution is indicated, and there are some hundreds of distribution maps; these are amended as more information becomes available, and there are yet others in process. These give only overall indications of natural - i.e. unaffected by recent human activities - distributions, and distributions on oceanic islands are usually very incomplete. In many cases the original outline maps on which many maps here are based have had to been amended, for instance, as substantial holes in the distributions of many apparently widely-ranging families have become apparent - indeed, it has proved surprisingly difficult to find/make accurate maps. Major resources include Hultén and Fries (1986: see also Hultén's earlier work), van Steenis (1963), van Steenis and van Balgooy (1966), van Balgooy (1975, 1984, 1993), Meusel and his collaborators (Meusel et al. 1965, 1978, 1992), and Quian and Ricklefs (2004: see electronic appendix, corrections of the often rather vague maps in Heywood [1978]); invaluable maps for tropical Africa are appearing, see Lebrun and Stork (2003 onwards). Some maps in Heywood et al. (2007) have been used as a last resort. There are various online resouces, including the excellent [FloraBase](javascript:showImage('http://florabase.calm.wa.gov.au',600,500)), for the flora of West Australia, and [Australia's Virtual Herbarium](javascript:showImage('http://avh.chah.org.au/',600,500)), for the flora of Australia as a whole; [BONAP's Taxonomic Data Center](javascript:showImage('http://bonap.net/tdc',600,500)) for the north American flora, also provides a useful check on the distributions of plants given in general maps (and also much else). Maps generated by searches on GBIF and Tropicos can be helpful, but beware of records from cultivated plants and aliens. I have included the distributions of fossils when they clarify the distributions of extant taxa. Sources for the maps are indicated.

总体分布情况已经说明，还有数百份分布图; 随着更多信息的获得，这些分布图将得到修正，还有一些正在处理中。这些数据只能全面说明自然情况——即不受最近人类活动影响的自然情况——的分布情况，而且在海洋岛屿上的分布情况通常很不完整。例如，在许多情况下，这里许多地图所依据的原先的轮廓地图不得不修改，因为许多看来分布广泛的家庭的分布出现了明显的漏洞——事实证明，要找到/制作准确的地图出人意料地困难。主要资源包括 Hultén 和 Fries (1986年: 参见 Hultén 的早期工作) ，van Steenis (1963年) ，van Steenis 和 van Balgooy (1966年) ，van Balgooy (1975年，1984年，1993年) ，Meusel 和他的合作者(Meusel et al. 1965年，1978年，1992年) ，Quian 和 Ricklefs(2004年: 参见电子附录，对海伍德常常相当模糊的地图的更正[1978])非洲热带地区的无价地图正在出现，见 Lebrun 和 Stork (2003年以后)。在海伍德等人(2007)的一些地图已经被用作最后的手段。有各种各样的在线资源，包括优秀的西澳大利亚植物志，和澳大利亚的虚拟植物标本，为整个澳大利亚的植物区系; BONAP 的北美植物分类数据中心，也提供了一个有用的检查分布的植物在一般地图(还有许多其他)。通过 GBIF 和 Tropicos 上的搜索生成的地图可能会有帮助，但要小心来自栽培植物和外星人的记录。在阐明现存分类群的分布时，我把化石的分布也包括在内。标明了地图的来源。

Following most families and a very few orders is a brief paragraph with features that may help in their recognition; the terms used here may not be perfectly "correct" botanically. Some of these features are taken from LaFrankie (2011), while Utteridge and Bramley (2014) suggest how the commoner tropical families can best be recognized.

跟随大多数家族和极少数订单的是一个简短的段落，其特征可能有助于识别它们; 这里使用的术语在植物学上可能并不完全“正确”。其中一些特征取自 LaFrankie (2011) ，而 Utteridge 和 Bramley (2014)则表明了如何最好地识别平民热带家庭。

There are a number of sections with subheadings following the family accounts (and also at other nodes when relevant), and most of these were introduced starting in late 2008. **Age** refers to crown-group ages, and these are placed at the appropriate node. In several cases there are substantially different age estimates for the same event, so treat these dates with particular caution. **Evolution** includes discussion on diversification and biogeography (Diversification & Distribution), comments on mycorrhizae and photosynthetic variants, etc. (Ecology & Physiology), information about pollination and disseminule distribution (Pollination Biology & Seed Dispersal), herbivory and galling (Plant/Animal Interactions), fungal and bacterial associations in general (Bacterial/Fungal Associations), interesting Vegetative Variation, Genes & Genomes, and plants with particular **Economic Importance**. Parts of these sections have also found their way to the section on [the evolution and diversification of the angiosperms](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/amborellalesweb2.htm#Evolution).

有一些章节在家庭账户之后有副标题(相关的时候也在其他节点) ，其中大部分是从2008年末开始引入的。年龄是指冠组的年龄，这些是放在适当的节点。在一些情况下，对同一事件的年龄估计存在很大差异，因此要特别谨慎对待这些日期。进化包括讨论多样化和生物地理学(多样化和分布) ，评论菌根和光合变异体等(生态学和生理学) ，关于授粉和散播分布(授粉生物学和种子传播) ，植食性和枯萎(植物/动物相互作用) ，真菌和细菌的一般组合(细菌/真菌组合) ，有趣的变异，基因和基因组，以及具有特殊经济意义的植物。这些剖面的一部分也找到了被子植物进化和多样化剖面。

In **Chemistry, Morphology, etc.** interesting variation within the family is summarized and there are references to sources of information that have been used but are not mentioned elsewhere in the family notes; there are additional general references in ["Characters"](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/characters.htm). Remember that many of the older "family" and "order" references include information about other groups some of which would not now be considered at all close. **Phylogeny** includes summaries of major works bearing on our current ideas of phylogentic relationships in the family. **Classification** includes references to the infrafamilial classification followed here, and there is often some discussion about generic limits. Earlier ideas of relationships (see **Previous Relationships**) includes largely some mention of some suggestions of Cronquist (1981) and Takhtajan (1997), but only because their work is still used. Finding out who was "first" in suggesting a particular relationship is no goal of these pages, the more so since what is often more interesting is not that a particular suggestion was made, but exactly why it was made. **Trivia** needs no explanation. The ["Bibliography"](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/referencesa_d.html) may still have holes.

在《化学》、《形态学》等书中，概述了家族内部有趣的变化，并提到了已经使用但在家族说明其他地方没有提到的信息来源; 在《人物》中还提到了其他一般性的参考资料。请记住，许多较老的“家庭”和“秩序”参考包括关于其他群体的信息，其中一些群体现在根本不会被考虑。系统发育学包括与我们目前关于家族系统发育关系的观念有关的主要著作的总结。分类包括对此后家族以下分类的参考，并且经常有关于类属界限的讨论。关于关系的早期观点(见以前的关系)主要包括一些克朗奎斯特(1981)和塔克塔詹(1997)的建议，但只是因为他们的作品仍在使用。找出谁是“第一个”提出某种特定关系的人并不是本文的目标，更有意思的是，往往更有意思的不是提出了某种特定的建议，而是提出这种建议的确切原因。琐事不需要解释。“参考书目”可能仍有漏洞。

In the ["Glossary"](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/glossarya_h.html#Glossary) there are definitions of the terms commonly used in the site and some other terms that may be encountered, representative chemical formulae, etc.. Definitions as far as possible follow current usage, rather than etymology or original definitions (see, e.g. Rickett 1954-56). Building this glossary has forced me to confront head-on such problems as the plethora of terms used to describe inflorescences (in part resolvable, I think, providing one does not attempt too much detail) and fruits (more difficult). Botany needs a common language, and for this the botanical community as a whole needs to agree on definitions. **A goal of botanical terminology must be to simplify the terms we use and to try and reduce the number of synonyms in common use.**

在「词汇表」内，载有本网站常用词汇的定义，以及可能遇到的其他词汇，具代表性的化学公式等。定义尽可能遵循当前的用法，而不是词源学或最初的定义(例如，Rickett 1954-56)。建立这个词汇表迫使我直面一些问题，比如描述花序的词汇过多(我认为部分可以解决，提供一个不要尝试太多细节)和水果(更难)。植物学需要一个共同的语言，为此，植物学界作为一个整体需要在定义上达成一致。植物学术语的一个目标必须是简化我们使用的术语，并试图减少常用的同义词的数量。

**!!IMPORTANT - WARNING TO ALL USERS!!**
[Back to Top](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/introductionnew.htm#top)

! ! 重要-警告所有用户!

All clades are hypotheses of relationships, and as hypotheses they may be overturned. Even though I have for the most part been conservative, changes in our ideas of relationships, and hence in the clades we talk about, are still likely in places. Relationships of a few taxa are still largely unknown or only partly known, and there will turn out to be a few seriously misplaced genera. Thus some changes are to be expected, but change is neither a defect of cladistics nor a necessary consequence of the use of molecular data.

所有的族群都是关于关系的假设，作为假设，它们可能被推翻。尽管我在很大程度上是保守的，但我们对人际关系的观念，以及我们所谈论的族群，仍然可能在某些地方发生变化。一些分类群的关系在很大程度上仍然是未知的或只是部分已知的，并且将会有一些严重错位的属。因此，一些变化是可以预期的，但变化既不是分支学的缺陷，也不是使用分子数据的必然结果。

A very important issue for all morphological studies, particularly at this level, is the documentation of variation within a character and the justification of the states that are used to describe this variation. As I often mention, the states used have frequently been inadequately justified, explicit criteria for their delimitation not having been presented. **Character states that lack justification may or may not compromise phylogenetic analyses, but there is certainly little reason to talk about their evolution** (Stevens 2000 for literature; see also [above](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/introductionnew.htm#Warning)). To quote Heywood (1973: p. 311) slightly out of context, "Systematics can be likened to a mincing machine into which data of all sorts is fed and processed to form a series of sausages ... The basic recipe for the construction of these "sausages" is usually secret, yet it is such encapsulated pieces of information that we have to work with and communicate with." In general, character states as conventionally delimited may not be as helpful to us as we might like or assume.

对于所有的形态学研究来说，尤其是在这个层次上，一个非常重要的问题是一个字符内部变异的记录，以及用来描述这种变异的状态的合理性。正如我经常提到的，使用的国家常常没有充分的理由，明确的标准，其划界没有提出。特征表明缺乏正当理由可能会或可能不会损害系统发育分析，但肯定没有什么理由谈论他们的进化(史蒂文斯2000文学; 也见上文)。引用海伍德(1973: p. 311)的话有点脱离上下文，“系统学可以比作一台切碎机器，将各种各样的数据输入和处理，形成一系列香肠... ... 构建这些“香肠”的基本配方通常是秘密的，但它是如此封装的信息，我们必须与之合作和沟通。”一般来说，按照惯例界定的性格状态对我们来说可能没有我们想象的那么有帮助。

For many characters in the characterizations our basic knowledge is often incomplete, and certainly sampling within families is often inadequate. However, I have included less information about chemical, wood anatomical, palynological, and embryological characters than I might. This is because for chemical characters (for example), my basic knowledge needs improving, while for some of the other more cryptic characters the sampling may be poor. But equally importantly, these notes began as teaching notes, and I judged that there was more than enough for the student or even the teacher to be going on with. An ideal system would include much more detail, the user ignoring anything irrelevant for the purpose at hand.

对于许多特征的描述，我们的基本知识往往是不完整的，当然抽样在家庭往往是不充分的。然而，我所包含的有关化学、木材解剖学、孢粉学和胚胎学特征的信息比我可能包含的要少。这是因为对于化学性状(例如) ，我的基本知识需要提高，而对于其他一些较为隐蔽的性状，抽样可能很差。但同样重要的是，这些笔记开始时是教学笔记，我判断学生甚至老师都有足够的笔记。理想的系统应该包括更多的细节，用户忽略与手头目的无关的任何东西。

That I mention some features as not being known is in many cases simply an expression of my ignorance.

我提到一些不为人知的特征，在许多情况下只是表达了我的无知。

This site is updated on a more or less continuous basis. I teach plant families at least every other year and that is a particularly good time for finding areas that need attention.

这个网站或多或少是连续更新的。我至少每隔一年教授一次植物家族，这是寻找需要关注领域的特别好时机。

*I am always more than grateful if you can let me know of any references in the text that lack citations, errors of omission or commission, etc.* - [peter.stevens@mobot.org](mailto:peter.stevens@mobot.org) should find me.

如果你能让我知道文本中任何缺少引用、遗漏或委托的错误的参考资料，我将非常感激，等等-peter.stevens@mobot. org 会找到我。

Spelling is erratic and somewhat mid-Atlantic; grammar is little better. All errors are mine.

拼写不规则，有点大西洋中部; 语法也好不到哪里去。所有的错误都是我的。

**HISTORY OF THE SITE**
[Back to Top](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/introductionnew.htm#top)

该地点的历史[返回页首]

These notes began as I taught Biology 103, the basic plant families course, at Harvard, taking over from Carroll E. Wood, Jr. (an impossible task). They became more wide-ranging when I twice taught OTS "Tropical Plant Systematics", and when I attempted to deal with all families in a one-semester, graduate-level course at Harvard. This last was a failure; we did not get to the monocots. However, the time and energy spent in assembling material for each class from all corners of the herbarium convinced me like nothing else could have that the modified Englerian system the herbarium then followed was didactically a disaster. Finally, I have long been interested in sight identification of herbarium material; unidentified specimens have to be brought into the system somehow. I have done this intermittently, but as frequently as I could, over the years, often with students and others, and this has been invaluable both in reviewing characters and also in learning more.

这些笔记开始于我在哈佛大学教授基础植物家族课程生物103的时候，接替了小卡罗尔 · 伍德(这是一项不可能完成的任务)。当我两次教授 OTS“热带植物分类学”时，当我试图在哈佛大学一个学期的研究生水平课程中与所有家庭打交道时，它们变得更加广泛。最后一个是失败的，我们没有进入单子叶植物。然而，我花费了大量的时间和精力从植物标本馆的各个角落为每一类植物组装材料，这让我确信，当时植物标本馆所遵循的改良的 Englerian 系统是一场灾难。最后，我一直对植物标本室的鉴定感兴趣，不明标本必须以某种方式进入系统。这些年来，我断断续续地做这些事情，尽可能频繁地与学生和其他人一起做这些事情，这在回顾人物和学习更多方面都是非常宝贵的。

The first version of the website (version 2) that was made generally known included literature that appeared as late as early August, 2001; the Introduction to this version is dated the 13th of July 2001. Version 2 benefited from teaching again in Costa Rica. This time I was with InBio personnel, and I learned perhaps more than I taught; a course given at the University of Campinas, in Brasil, was similarly stimulating.

该网站的第一个版本(第2版)广为人知，其中包括2001年8月初出版的文献; 该版本的导言日期为2001年7月13日。第二版再次受益于哥斯达黎加的教学。这一次我在 InBio 人事部，学到的东西可能比我教的还多; 在巴西的坎皮纳斯州立大学开设的一门课程也同样令人兴奋。

**THE FUTURE**
[Back to Top](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/introductionnew.htm#top)

未来[返回页首]

What happens with these pages depends on how useful they are found to be, or can be made to be. Their goal is to help in teaching, although I find them also a useful research tool in that they help direct one's attention to interesting characters and to taxa that are poorly understood. They are not intended to compete with other web sites that depict the tree of life, etc.

这些页面发生了什么，取决于它们被发现有多有用，或者可以被制作成多有用。他们的目标是帮助教学，虽然我发现他们也是一个有用的研究工具，因为他们帮助引导人们的注意力到有趣的人物和分类是很少了解。他们并不打算与其他描绘生命之树的网站竞争，等等。

Filling in gaps in the literature continues to improve family characterisations; three character systems in particular, chemistry, wood anatomy and palynology, clearly need more attention. We will continue to build in more links to photographs and to other web sites, particularly those that focus on families. Adding good diagrams showing the basic floral morphology of each family would be very helpful (see Ronse DeCraene 2010 for recent work on floral diagrams; Eichler 1875-1878 remains invaluable), and simple floral formulae are being added, although complex formulae can be difficult to understand (see Prenner et al. 2010; Simpson 2010; Nuraliev et al. 2019 for other symbols that might be useful).

填补文献的空白继续改善家族特征，特别是三个字符系统，化学，木材解剖学和孢粉学，显然需要更多的注意。我们将继续建立更多照片和其他网站的链接，特别是那些关注家庭的网站。添加良好的图表显示每个家庭的花的基本形态学将是非常有帮助的(见 Ronse DeCraene 2010最近的工作花图; Eichler 1875-1878仍然是宝贵的) ，简单的花公式正在被添加，虽然复杂的公式可能难以理解(见 Prenner 等人2010; Simpson 2010; Nuraliev 等人2019可能有用的其他符号)。

**THANKS**
[Back to Top](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/top/introductionnew.htm#top)

谢谢[返回页首]

Last, but certainly not least, I thank Kobinah Abdul-Salim, Stuart Davies, Diane Ferguson, Rick Ree, George Weiblen and Barbara Whitlock for providing the impetus to start this. Students at courses at Harvard University, Massachusetts, InBio, Costa Rica, the University of Campinas, Brasil, and the University of Missouri, St Louis and Missouri Botanical Garden have worked with successive versions of the hierarchy, uncovering flaws as they did do; to them my thanks for their enthusiasm and tolerance. Librarians at Harvard University and the Missouri Botanical Garden have been unfailingly helpful in finding sometimes obscure references. A few sections have been read by colleagues who are thanked individually in the text. Many people have sent in comments and/or noticed mistakes; my thanks to you all, although I have not mentioned you individually unless you have caught particularly egregious errors! Mark Olson, Beth Owen and Bob Magill helped to set up the site. Finally, to say that I am extremely grateful to Hilary Davis for building the site, adding the links to the Gentry photographs of the Missouri Botanical Garden, and generally helping things along, is an understatement.

最后，但肯定不是最不重要的，我感谢 Kobinah Abdul-Salim，Stuart Davies，Diane Ferguson，Rick Ree，George Weiblen 和 Barbara Whitlock，感谢他们提供了开始这个项目的动力。在哈佛大学、马萨诸塞州、 InBio、哥斯达黎加、坎皮纳斯州立大学、巴西、密苏里大学、圣路易斯和密苏里植物园的学生们，他们在不同版本的等级制度下工作，发现了他们所做的缺陷; 我要感谢他们的热情和宽容。哈佛大学和密苏里植物园的图书管理员一直在帮助寻找一些模糊的参考资料。同事们宣读了其中的一些章节，并在案文中对他们个别表示感谢。许多人发来了评论和/或注意到了错误; 我感谢你们所有人，虽然我没有单独提到你们，除非你们发现了特别严重的错误！马克 · 奥尔森，贝丝 · 欧文和鲍勃 · 马吉尔帮助建立了这个网站。最后，要说我非常感谢 Hilary Davis 建立了这个网站，添加了密苏里植物园的 Gentry 照片的链接，总的来说帮助了很多事情，这是一个轻描淡写的说法。

P. F. Stevens, 13 (Friday) July 2001 - University of Missouri, St Louis, and Missouri Botanical Garden.

2001年7月13日(星期五)-密苏里大学，圣路易斯和密苏里植物园。

**Version 2**.

第二版。

I inexcusably forgot to thank Dr Barry Hammel (Costa Rica) and Drs Maria Amaral and Volker Bittrich (Campinas, Brasil) for their invitations to teach/learn from InBio personnel and University of Campinas staff and students respectively. For version 3, many have been kind in either giving us their photographs or allowing us to make direct links to their photographs: Atlas of Florida Vascular Plants, Arizona State University Herbarium, Australian National Botanic Gardens, David Boufford - Biodiversity of the Hengduan Mountains China, Mark Brand - UConn Plant Database, CalPhotos, Connecticut Botanical Society, Michael Dillon - Andean Botanical Information System, Michael A. Dirr, Murray Fagg - Australian National Botanic Gardens, Gardenweek.org, Christine Howells - Australian Plants Society Tasmania, Kelly Irvin - International Bulb Society, Don Les, John Maunder - Provincial Museum of Newfoundland and Labrador, Kate McCombs - Christchurch City Council New Zealand, Andrew Morgan - University of Tasmania, Clinton Morse - University of Connecticut Greenhouse, Mount Tomah Botanic Garden Australia, Lytton J. Musselman, Dan Nickrent - Parasitic Plant Connection, Plant of the Week - Smithsonian Institution, James Reveal, George Schatz - Madagascar Conspectus Website, Thomas Schöpke, Tim Stephens - University of California Santa Cruz, Kurt Stüber, Jim Mann Taylor, Texas A&M Bioinformatics Working Group Vascular Plant Gallery, Brian Walters - Australian Society for Growing Native Australian Plants, Len Webb Ecological Images Collection, Western Australia Seagrass Website, Steven J. Wolf, University of Wisconsin Plant Systematics Collection. Gerald Carr and Heinz Schneider have been particularly generous in making available many magnificent photographs; these are but some that can be found at the sites that the two maintain ([Vascular Plant Families Image Gallery](javascript:showImage('http://www.botany.hawaii.edu/faculty/carr/phylo_fpfamilies.htm',600,500)) and [Botanical Image Database](javascript:showImage('http://www.unibas.ch/botimage/fame.htm',600,500)), respectively). Dave Boufford has caught many errors throughout the site, as has Paul von Rijckevorsel. I am again grateful to students at the University of Missouri at St Louis, Washington University, and St Louis University, and to staff and visitors at the Missouri Botanical Garden. And once again, my sincere thanks to Hilary Davis, to whom the improvements of the site are due.

我不可原谅地忘记感谢 Barry Hammel 博士(哥斯达黎加)和 Maria Amaral 博士和 Volker Bittrich 博士(巴西 Campinas)邀请他们分别向 InBio 人事部和坎皮纳斯州立大学的教职员工和学生进行教学。对于第三版，许多人友好地给了我们他们的照片，或者允许我们直接链接到他们的照片: 佛罗里达维管植物地图集，亚利桑那州立大学植物标本室，澳洲国家植物园，David Boufford-中国横断山脉的生物多样性,马克 · 布兰德-康涅狄格州立大学植物数据库，康涅狄格州植物学会，迈克尔 · 狄龙-安第斯植物信息系统，迈克尔 · a · 迪尔，Murray Fagg-澳洲国家植物园，gardenweek. org，Christine Howells-Australian Plants Society Tasmania，Kelly Irvin-International Bulb Society，Don Les,新西兰克赖斯特彻奇市议会，纽芬兰-拉布拉多塔斯马尼亚大学，克林顿莫尔斯康涅狄格大学温室,生物信息学工作组维管植物图片史密森尼学会,澳大利亚原生植物种植协会，Len Webb 生态图片收藏，西澳大利亚海草网站，Steven j. Wolf，威斯康星大学麦迪逊分校植物系统收藏。杰拉尔德 · 卡尔和海因茨 · 施耐德特别慷慨地提供了许多壮观的照片，但这些只是在他们两人维护的遗址(分别是维管植物家族图片库和植物图片数据库)中发现的一些。戴夫 · 布福德在网站上发现了许多错误，保罗 · 冯 · 里克沃塞尔也是如此。我再次感谢圣路易斯密苏里大学、华盛顿大学和圣路易斯大学的学生，以及密苏里植物园的工作人员和访客。并再次，我真诚地感谢希拉里戴维斯，她的网站的改进是由于。

P. F. Stevens, 15 May 2002 - University of Missouri, St Louis, and Missouri Botanical Garden.

史蒂文斯，2002年5月15日-密苏里大学，圣路易斯和密苏里植物园。

第三版。

Once again, the normal list of suspects is to be thanked. Many people have written in with comments that, whether apparently trivial or cosmic, I have tried to take into account. I remain grateful to students at the University of Missouri at St Louis, Washington University, and St Louis University, and to staff and visitors at the Missouri Botanical Garden. Hilary Davis continues to improve the site.

正常的嫌疑人名单再一次得到了感谢。许多人在评论中写道，无论是显然微不足道的还是宇宙万物，我都试图将其考虑在内。我仍然感谢圣路易斯，华盛顿大学和圣路易斯大学密苏里大学的学生，以及密苏里植物园的工作人员和访客。希拉里 · 戴维斯继续改进网站。

**Version 5**.

第五版。

Version 5 is being archived today, Sunday May 22. All those who have caught mistakes and made suggestions are gratefully thanked, and Hilary Davis is particularly thanked for developing the protocol for making the maps. She has also developed a protocol for integrating illustrations of critical characters with the text that we will try and implement this next year.

5月22日星期天，5号版本将被存档。我们感谢所有发现错误并提出建议的人，并特别感谢希拉里 · 戴维斯为绘制这些地图制定了方案。她还制定了一个协议，将关键字符的插图与文本结合起来，我们明年将尝试实施这一协议。

P. F. Stevens, 22 May 2005 - University of Missouri, St Louis, and Missouri Botanical Garden.

史蒂文斯，2005年5月22日-密苏里大学，圣路易斯和密苏里植物园。

**Version 6**.

第六版。

Version 6 was archived on Sunday May 21. All those who have caught mistakes and made suggestions are gratefully thanked, and Andrew Ford has been particularly helpful. The library staff at the Missouri Botanical Garden have patiently dealt with a positive barrage of queries this last year, and I thank Victoria McMichael and Mary Stiffler in particular for their tolerance. Hilary Davies continues to help developing the site.

版本6在5月21日星期天被存档。我们感谢所有发现错误并提出建议的人，安德鲁 · 福特对我们尤其有帮助。去年，密苏里植物园图书馆的工作人员耐心地处理了一连串积极的询问，我特别感谢 Victoria McMichael 和 Mary Stiffler 的宽容。希拉里 · 戴维斯继续帮助开发这个网站。

P. F. Stevens, 22 May 2006 - University of Missouri, St Louis, and Missouri Botanical Garden.

史蒂文斯，2006年5月22日-密苏里大学，圣路易斯和密苏里植物园。

**Version 7**.

第七版。

Version 7 was archived on Sunday, June 3. I am particularly grateful to students in my plant families course for making this last term so stimulating, and spurring the development of a new section of the site, the ["Student"](http://www.mobot.org/MOBOT/Research/APweb/orders/Introstudent.html#Introduction) section, which Hilary Davis put up just prior to archiving. Again, the library staff have been swamped with requests, and again corrections and additions have been suggested; I thank all who have been involved in this project, no matter how apparently peripherally.

7版本于6月3日星期日存档。我特别感谢参加我的植物家庭课程的学生们，他们使最后一个学期如此令人兴奋，并促进了网站新部分的开发——“学生”部分，这是希拉里 · 戴维斯在存档之前建立的。再一次，图书馆工作人员已经被请求淹没，再一次的修正和增加已经被建议; 我感谢所有参与这个项目的人，不管是多么明显的边缘。

P. F. Stevens, 8 June 2007 - University of Missouri, St Louis, and Missouri Botanical Garden.

史蒂文斯，2007年6月8日-密苏里大学，圣路易斯和密苏里植物园。

**Version 8**.

12版本于7月25日存档。整个网站正在被修改的过程中，这暴露了在很长一段时间里零零星星地添加一些信息的后果... 此外，在 Cam 的帮助下，已经给出了 xml 标记，其中许多是在去年添加的，这些标记将很快扩展到讨论、节点等等。感谢艾米、费利佩和希拉里的持续帮助，花园图书馆的工作人员比平时更多地接二连三地提出要求，感谢沃尔克 · 比特里希和你们所有人的评论和更正。

P. F. Stevens, Tuesday, August 1, 2012 \- University of Missouri, St Louis, and Missouri Botanical Garden.

2012年8月1日，星期二\-圣路易斯密苏里大学和密苏里植物园。

**Version 13**.

版本13。

Version 12 was archived on September 26th. The reworking of the site has continued \- apomorphies have now been flagged throughout the site, and dates for clades, which were in a considerable mess, are being cleaned up. Given the reorganisation of the site over the last couple of years, the "Student" section has been removed, as has the "Apomorphies" section (it is now redundant) and the "Statistics" section (that was simply one more area to keep up to date, and anyhow, I had largely ignored it).

12版本于9月26日存档。网站的重新工作已经连续\-非标记的营养现在已标记整个网站，和日期的分支，这是一个相当大的混乱，正在清理。考虑到过去几年网站的重组，“学生”部分已经被删除，“ apomorepies”部分(现在是多余的)和“统计”部分(这只是另一个需要更新的区域，无论如何，我基本上忽略了它)也被删除了。

P. F. Stevens, Tuesday, September 28, 2013 \- University of Missouri, St Louis, and Missouri Botanical Garden.

2013年9月28日，星期二，圣路易斯密苏里大学和密苏里植物园。

**Version 14**.

版本14。

Getting there.... Dates for clades are now largely cleaned up, but most must be seriously inaccurate. The next push must be to clean up the trees. Readers have made many useful comments, and Felipe Zapata in particular has helped with literature.

到达那里... ..。现在基本上清理了支序的日期，但大多数日期肯定严重不准确。下一步必须是清理树木。读者提出了许多有用的意见，尤其是费利佩 · 萨帕塔在文学方面帮了大忙。

P. F. Stevens, July 4, 2017 \- University of Missouri, St Louis, and Missouri Botanical Garden.

史蒂文斯，2017年7月4日\-密苏里大学，圣路易斯和密苏里植物园。
